## Numerics: A.P & G.P

**Q1. 587 x 999 = ?**

- **A.** 586413  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 587523
- **C.** 614823
- **D.** 615173

**Explanation:** 587 x 999 = 587 x (1000 - 1) = 587 x 1000 - 587 x 1 = 587000 - 587 = 586413.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001022](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001022)*

---

**Q2. (?) - 19657 - 33994 = 9999**

- **A.** 63650  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 53760
- **C.** 59640
- **D.** 61560

**Explanation:** 19657 Let x - 53651 = 9999 33994 Then, x = 9999 + 53651 = 63650 ----- 53651 -----

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001004](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001004)*

**Q3. A number when divided successively by 4 and 5 leaves remainders 1 and 4 respectively. When it is successively divided by 5 and 4, then the respective remainders will be**

- **A.** 1, 2
- **B.** 2, 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 3, 2
- **D.** 4, 1

**Explanation:** 4 | x y = (5 x 1 + 4) = 9 -------- 5 | y -1 x = (4 x y + 1) = (4 x 9 + 1) = 37 -------- | 1 -4 Now, 37 when divided successively by 5 and 4, we get 5 | 37 --------- 4 | 7 - 2 --------- | 1 - 3 Respective remainders are 2 and 3.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001027](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001027)*

---

**Q4. (112 x 5 4 ) = ?**

- **A.** 67000
- **B.** 70000  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 76500
- **D.** 77200

**Explanation:** (112 x 5 4 ) = 112 x 10 4 = 112 x 10 4 = 1120000 = 70000 2 2 4 16

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001001)*

**Q6. The sum of first 45 natural numbers is:**

- **A.** 1035  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 1280
- **C.** 2070
- **D.** 2140

**Explanation:** Let S n = (1 + 2 + 3 + ... + 45) This is an A.P. in which a = 1, d = 1, n = 45 and l = 45 S n = n ( a + l ) = 45 x (1 + 45) = (45 x 23) = 1035 2 2 Required sum = 1035.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001024](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001024)*

**Q7. Which one of the following can't be the square of natural number ?**

- **A.** 32761
- **B.** 81225
- **C.** 42437  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 20164

**Explanation:** The square of a natural number never ends in 7. 42437 is not the square of a natural number.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001023](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001023)*

**Q8. 35 + 15 x 1.5 = ?**

- **A.** 85
- **B.** 51.5
- **C.** 57.5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 5.25

**Explanation:** Given Exp. = 35 + 15 x 3 = 35 + 45 = 35 + 22.5 = 57.5 2 2

**Q9. 106 x 106 - 94 x 94 = ?**

- **A.** 2400  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 2000
- **C.** 1904
- **D.** 1906

**Explanation:** 106 x 106 - 94 x 94 = (106) 2 - (94) 2 = (106 + 94)(106 - 94) [ Ref: (a 2 - b 2 ) = (a + b)(a - b) ] = (200 x 12) = 2400.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026)*

---

**Q10. Which of the following numbers will completely divide (4 61 + 4 62 + 4 63 + 4 64 ) ?**

- **A.** 3
- **B.** 10  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 11
- **D.** 13

**Explanation:** (4 61 + 4 62 + 4 63 + 4 64 ) = 4 61 x (1 + 4 + 4 2 + 4 3 ) = 4 61 x 85 = 4 60 x (4 x 85) = (4 60 x 340), which is divisible by 10.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026)*

---

**Q11. Which of the following number is divisible by 24 ?**

- **A.** 35718
- **B.** 63810
- **C.** 537804
- **D.** 3125736  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** 24 = 3 x8, where 3 and 8 co-prime. Clearly, 35718 is not divisible by 8, as 718 is not divisible by 8. Similarly, 63810 is not divisible by 8 and 537804 is not divisible by 8. Consider option (D), Sum of digits = (3 + 1 + 2 + 5 + 7 + 3 + 6) = 27, which is divisible by 3. Also, 736 is divisible by 8. 3125736 is divisible by (3 x 8), i.e., 24.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001005](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001005)*

---

**Q12. It is being given that (2 32 + 1) is completely divisible by a whole number. Which of the following numbers is completely divisible by this number?**

- **A.** (2 16 + 1)
- **B.** (2 16 - 1)
- **C.** (7 x 2 23 )
- **D.** (2 96 + 1)  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let 2 32 = x . Then, (2 32 + 1) = ( x + 1). Let ( x + 1) be completely divisible by the natural number N. Then, (2 96 + 1) = [(2 32 ) 3 + 1] = ( x 3 + 1) = ( x + 1)( x 2 - x + 1), which is completely divisible by N, since ( x + 1) is divisible by N.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001001)*

---

**Q13. If the number 653 xy is divisible by 90, then ( x + y ) = ?**

- **A.** 2
- **B.** 3
- **C.** 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 6

**Explanation:** 90 = 10 x 9 Clearly, 653 xy is divisible by 10, so y = 0 Now, 653 x 0 is divisible by 9. So, (6 + 5 + 3 + x + 0) = (14 + x ) is divisible by 9. So, x = 4. Hence, ( x + y ) = (4 + 0) = 4.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026)*

---

**Q14. If the number 517*324 is completely divisible by 3, then the smallest whole number in the place of * will be:**

- **A.** 0
- **B.** 1
- **C.** 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Sum of digits = (5 + 1 + 7 + x + 3 + 2 + 4) = (22 + x ), which must be divisible by 3. x = 2.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001004](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001004)*

**Q15. 107 x 107 + 93 x 93 = ?**

- **A.** 19578
- **B.** 19418
- **C.** 20098  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 21908

**Explanation:** 107 x 107 + 93 x 93 = (107) 2 + (93) 2 = (100 + 7) 2 + (100 - 7) 2 = 2 x [(100) 2 + 7 2 ] [ Ref: (a + b) 2 + (a - b) 2 = 2(a 2 + b 2 ) ] = 20098

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006)*

**Q16. (963 + 476) 2 + (963 - 476) 2 = ? (963 x 963 + 476 x 476)**

- **A.** 1449
- **B.** 497
- **C.** 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 4

**Explanation:** Given Exp. = ( a + b ) 2 + ( a - b ) 2 = 2( a 2 + b 2 ) = 2 ( a 2 + b 2 ) ( a 2 + b 2 )

**Q17. The difference between the local value and the face value of 7 in the numeral 32675149 is**

- **A.** 75142
- **B.** 64851
- **C.** 5149
- **D.** 69993  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** (Local value of 7) - (Face value of 7) = (70000 - 7) = 69993

**Q18. What is the unit digit in 7 105 ?**

- **A.** 1
- **B.** 5
- **C.** 7  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 9

**Explanation:** Unit digit in 7 105 = Unit digit in [ (7 4 ) 26 x 7 ] But, unit digit in (7 4 ) 26 = 1 Unit digit in 7 105 = (1 x 7) = 7

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001026)*

**Q19. How many of the following numbers are divisible by 132 ? 264, 396, 462, 792, 968, 2178, 5184, 6336**

- **A.** 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 5
- **C.** 6
- **D.** 7

**Explanation:** 132 = 4 x 3 x 11 So, if the number divisible by all the three number 4, 3 and 11, then the number is divisible by 132 also. 264 11,3,4 (/) 396 11,3,4 (/) 462 11,3 (X) 792 11,3,4 (/) 968 11,4 (X) 2178 11,3 (X) 5184 3,4 (X) 6336 11,3,4 (/) Therefore the following numbers are divisible by 132 : 264, 396, 792 and 6336. Required number of number = 4.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001002)*

**Q20. The sum of all two digit numbers divisible by 5 is:**

- **A.** 1035
- **B.** 1245
- **C.** 1230
- **D.** 945  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Required numbers are 10, 15, 20, 25, ..., 95 This is an A.P. in which a = 10, d = 5 and l = 95. t n = 95 a + ( n - 1) d = 95 10 + ( n - 1) x 5 = 95 ( n - 1) x 5 = 85 ( n - 1) = 17 n = 18 Requuired Sum = n ( a + l ) = 18 x (10 + 95) = (9 x 105) = 945. 2 2

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001024](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001024)*

---

**Q21. On dividing a number by 5, we get 3 as remainder. What will the remainder when the square of the this number is divided by 5 ?**

- **A.** 0
- **B.** 1
- **C.** 2
- **D.** 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the number be x and on dividing x by 5, we get k as quotient and 3 as remainder. x = 5k + 3 x 2 = (5k + 3) 2 = (25 k 2 + 30 k + 9) = 5(5 k 2 + 6 k + 1) + 4 On dividing x 2 by 5, we get 4 as remainder.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001007](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001007)*

**Q25. If n is a natural number, then (6 n 2 + 6 n ) is always divisible by:**

- **A.** 6 only
- **B.** 6 and 12 both  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 12 only
- **D.** by 18 only

**Explanation:** (6 n 2 + 6 n ) = 6 n ( n + 1), which is always divisible by 6 and 12 both, since n ( n + 1) is always even.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006)*

---

**Q26. The sum of first 45 natural numbers is:**

- **A.** 1035  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 1280
- **C.** 2070
- **D.** 2140

**Explanation:** Let S n =(1 + 2 + 3 + ... + 45). This is an A.P. in which a =1, d =1, n = 45. S n = n [2 a + ( n - 1) d ] = 45 x [2 x 1 + (45 - 1) x 1] = 45 x 46 = (45 x 23) 2 2 2 = 45 x (20 + 3) = 45 x 20 + 45 x 3 = 900 + 135 = 1035. Shorcut Method: S n = n ( n + 1) = 45(45 + 1) = 1035. 2 2

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001004](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001004)*

---

- **A.** 534
- **B.** 446
- **C.** 354
- **D.** 324  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Given Exp. = a 2 + b 2 - 2 ab , where a = 287 and b = 269 = ( a - b ) 2 = (287 - 269) 2 = (18 2 ) = 324

**Q28. How many natural numbers are there between 23 and 100 which are exactly divisible by 6 ?**

- **A.** 8
- **B.** 11
- **C.** 12
- **D.** 13  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Required numbers are 24, 30, 36, 42, ..., 96 This is an A.P. in which a = 24, d = 6 and l = 96 Let the number of terms in it be n . Then t n = 96 a + ( n - 1) d = 96 24 + ( n - 1) x 6 = 96 ( n - 1) x 6 = 72 ( n - 1) = 12 n = 13 Required number of numbers = 13.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001007](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001007)*

**Q36. The difference between a positive proper fraction and its reciprocal is 9/20. The fraction is:**

- **A.** 3 5
- **B.** 3 10
- **C.** 4 5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 4 3

**Explanation:** Let the required fraction be x . Then 1 - x = 9 x 20 1 - x 2 = 9 x 20 20 - 20 x 2 = 9 x 20 x 2 + 9 x - 20 = 0 20 x 2 + 25 x - 16 x - 20 = 0 5 x (4 x + 5) - 4(4 x + 5) = 0 (4 x + 5)(5 x - 4) = 0 x = 4 5

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006)*

---

**Q37. {(476 + 424) 2 - 4 x 476 x 424} = ?**

- **A.** 2906
- **B.** 3116
- **C.** 2704  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 2904

**Explanation:** Given Exp. = [( a + b ) 2 - 4 ab ], where a = 476 and b = 424 = [(476 + 424) 2 - 4 x 476 x 424] = [(900) 2 - 807296] = 810000 - 807296 = 2704.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001028](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001028)*

**Q38. 72519 x 9999 = ?**

- **A.** 725117481  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 674217481
- **C.** 685126481
- **D.** 696217481

**Explanation:** 72519 x 9999 = 72519 x (10000 - 1) = 72519 x 10000 - 72519 x 1 = 725190000 - 72519 = 725117481.

**Q39. (2 2 + 4 2 + 6 2 + ... + 20 2 ) = ?**

- **A.** 770
- **B.** 1155
- **C.** 1540  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 385 x 385

**Explanation:** (2 2 + 4 2 + 6 2 + ... + 20 2 ) = (1 x 2) 2 + (2 x 2) 2 + (2 x 3) 2 + ... + (2 x 10) 2 = (2 2 x 1 2 ) + (2 2 x 2 2 ) + (2 2 x 3 2 ) + ... + (2 2 x 10 2 ) = 2 2 x [1 2 + 2 2 + 3 2 + ... + 10 2 ] Ref: (1 2 + 2 2 + 3 2 + ... + n 2 ) = 1 n ( n + 1)(2 n + 1) 6 = 4 x 1 x 10 x 11 x 21 6 = (4 x 5 x 77) = 1540.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001023](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001023)*

**Q42. A number was divided successively in order by 4, 5 and 6. The remainders were respectively 2, 3 and 4. The number is:**

- **A.** 214  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 476
- **C.** 954
- **D.** 1908

**Explanation:** 4 | x z = 6 x 1 + 4 = 10 ----------- 5 | y -2 y = 5 x z + 3 = 5 x 10 + 3 = 53 ----------- 6 | z - 3 x = 4 x y + 2 = 4 x 53 + 2 = 214 ----------- | 1 - 4 Hence, required number = 214.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001022](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001022)*

---

**Q43. How many 3 digit numbers are divisible by 6 in all ?**

- **A.** 149
- **B.** 150  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 151
- **D.** 166

**Explanation:** Required numbers are 102, 108, 114, ... , 996 This is an A.P. in which a = 102, d = 6 and l = 996 Let the number of terms be n . Then, a + ( n - 1) d = 996 102 + ( n - 1) x 6 = 996 6 x ( n - 1) = 894 ( n - 1) = 149 n = 150.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001008](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001008)*

---

**Q44. On dividing a number by 56, we get 29 as remainder. On dividing the same number by 8, what will be the remainder ?**

- **A.** 4
- **B.** 5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 6
- **D.** 7

**Explanation:** Formula: (Divisor*Quotient) + Remainder = Dividend. Soln: (56*Q)+29 = D -------(1) D%8 = R -------------(2) From equation(2), ((56*Q)+29)%8 = R. => Assume Q = 1. => (56+29)%8 = R. => 85%8 = R => 5 = R.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001006)*

---

**Q45. A 3-digit number 4 a 3 is added to another 3-digit number 984 to give a 4-digit number 13 b 7, which is divisible by 11. Then, ( a + b ) = ?**

- **A.** 10  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 11
- **C.** 12
- **D.** 15

**Explanation:** 4 a 3 | 9 8 4 } ==> a + 8 = b ==> b - a = 8 13 b 7 | Also, 13 b 7 is divisible by 11 (7 + 3) - ( b + 1) = (9 - b ) (9 - b ) = 0 b = 9 ( b = 9 and a = 1) ( a + b ) = 10.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001008](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001008)*

---

- **A.** 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** (4 + 5 + 2) - (1 + 6 + 3) = 1, not divisible by 11. (2 + 6 + 4) - (4 + 5 + 2) = 1, not divisible by 11. (4 + 6 + 1) - (2 + 5 + 3) = 1, not divisible by 11. (4 + 6 + 1) - (2 + 5 + 4) = 0, So, 415624 is divisible by 11.

**Q72. What is the unit digit in the product (3 65 x 6 59 x 7 71 )?**

- **D.** 6

**Explanation:** Unit digit in 3 4 = 1 Unit digit in (3 4 ) 16 = 1 Unit digit in 3 65 = Unit digit in [ (3 4 ) 16 x 3 ] = (1 x 3) = 3 Unit digit in 6 59 = 6 Unit digit in 7 4 Unit digit in (7 4 ) 17 is 1. Unit digit in 7 71 = Unit digit in [(7 4 ) 17 x 7 3 ] = (1 x 3) = 3 Required digit = Unit digit in (3 x 6 x 3) = 4.

**Q73. The difference of the squares of two consecutive odd integers is divisible by which of the following integers ?**

- **A.** 3
- **B.** 6
- **C.** 7
- **D.** 8  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the two consecutive odd integers be (2 n + 1) and (2 n + 3). Then, (2 n + 3) 2 - (2 n + 1) 2 = (2 n + 3 + 2 n + 1) (2 n + 3 - 2 n - 1) = (4 n + 4) x 2 = 8( n + 1), which is divisible by 8.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001022](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001022)*

---

**Q74. It is being given that (2 32 + 1) is completely divisible by a whole number. Which of the following numbers is completely divisible by this number?**

- **A.** (2 16 + 1)
- **B.** (2 16 - 1)
- **C.** (7 x 2 23 )
- **D.** (2 96 + 1)  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let 2 32 = x . Then, (2 32 + 1) = ( x + 1). Let ( x + 1) be completely divisible by the natural number N. Then, (2 96 + 1) = [(2 32 ) 3 + 1] = ( x 3 + 1) = ( x + 1)( x 2 - x + 1), which is completely divisible by N, since ( x + 1) is divisible by N.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/)*

---

**Explanation:** Unit digit in (6374) 1793 = Unit digit in (4) 1793 = Unit digit in [(4 2 ) 896 x 4] = Unit digit in (6 x 4) = 4 Unit digit in (625) 317 = Unit digit in (5) 317 = 5 Unit digit in (341) 491 = Unit digit in (1) 491 = 1 Required digit = Unit digit in (4 x 5 x 1) = 0.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/numbers/001002)*

## Numerics: Area and Volume

**Q79. The area of a rectangle is equal to the area of right-angles triangle. What is the length of the rectangle? I. The base of the triangle is 40 cm. II. The height of the triangle is 50 cm.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Given: Area of rectangle = Area of a right-angles triangle. l x b = 1 x B x H 2 I gives, B = 40 cm. II gives, H = 50 cm. Thus, to find l , we need b also, which is not given. Given data is not sufficient to give the answer. Correct answer is (D).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/055001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/055001)*

---

**Q80. A metallic sheet is of rectangular shape with dimensions 48 m x 36 m. From each of its corners, a square is cut off so as to make an open box. If the length of the square is 8 m, the volume of the box (in m 3 ) is:**

- **A.** 4830
- **B.** 5120  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 6420
- **D.** 8960

**Explanation:** Clearly, l = (48 - 16)m = 32 m, b = (36 -16)m = 20 m, h = 8 m. Volume of the box = (32 x 20 x 8) m 3 = 5120 m 3 .

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002)*

---

**Q81. What is the area of the hall? I. Material cost of flooring per square metre is Rs. 2.50 II. Labour cost of flooring the hall is Rs. 3500 III. Total cost of flooring the hall is Rs. 14,500.**

- **A.** I and II only
- **B.** II and III only
- **C.** All I, II and III  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Any two of the three

**Explanation:** I. Material cost = Rs. 2.50 per m 2 II. Labour cost = Rs. 3500. III. Total cost = Rs. 14,500. Let the area be A sq. metres. Material cost = Rs. (14500 - 3500) = Rs. 11,000. 5A = 11000 A = 11000 x 2 = 4400 m 2 . 2 5 Thus, all I, II and III are needed to get the answer. Correct answer is (C).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/056001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/056001)*

---

**Q82. A hollow iron pipe is 21 cm long and its external diameter is 8 cm. If the thickness of the pipe is 1 cm and iron weighs 8 g/cm 3 , then the weight of the pipe is:**

- **A.** 3.6 kg
- **B.** 3.696 kg  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 36 kg
- **D.** 36.9 kg

**Explanation:** External radius = 4 cm, Internal radius = 3 cm. Volume of iron = 22 x [(4) 2 - (3) 2 ] x 21 cm 3 7 = 22 x 7 x 1 x 21 cm 3 7 = 462 cm 3 . Weight of iron = (462 x 8) gm = 3696 gm = 3.696 kg.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/)*

---

**Q83. An error 2% in excess is made while measuring the side of a square. The percentage of error in the calculated area of the square is:**

- **A.** 2%
- **B.** 2.02%
- **C.** 4%
- **D.** 4.04%  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** 100 cm is read as 102 cm. A 1 = (100 x 100) cm 2 and A 2 (102 x 102) cm 2 . (A 2 - A 1 ) = [(102) 2 - (100) 2 ] = (102 + 100) x (102 - 100) = 404 cm 2 . Percentage error = 404 x 100 % = 4.04% 100 x 100

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/)*

---

**Q84. What is the height of a circular cone? I. The area of that cone is equal to the area of a rectangle whose length is 33 cm. II. The area of the base of that cone is 154 sq. cm.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** II gives the value of r . But, in I, the breadth of rectangle is not given. So, we cannot find the surface area of the cone. Hence, the height of the cone cannot be determined. Correct answer is (D).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001)*

---

**Q85. In a shower, 5 cm of rain falls. The volume of water that falls on 1.5 hectares of ground is:**

- **A.** 75 cu. m
- **B.** 750 cu. m  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 7500 cu. m
- **D.** 75000 cu. m

**Explanation:** 1 hectare = 10,000 m 2 So, Area = (1.5 x 10000) m 2 = 15000 m 2 . Depth = 5 m = 1 m. 100 20 Volume = (Area x Depth) = 15000 x 1 m 3 = 750 m 3 . 20 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/dDbVuBzYop8

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058001)*

---

**Q86. A cistern 6m long and 4 m wide contains water up to a depth of 1 m 25 cm. The total area of the wet surface is:**

- **A.** 49 m 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 50 m 2
- **C.** 53.5 m 2
- **D.** 55 m 2

**Explanation:** Area of the wet surface = [2( lb + bh + lh ) - lb ] = 2( bh + lh ) + lb = [2 (4 x 1.25 + 6 x 1.25) + 6 x 4] m 2 = 49 m 2 .

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002)*

---

**Q87. The ratio between the length and the breadth of a rectangular park is 3 : 2. If a man cycling along the boundary of the park at the speed of 12 km/hr completes one round in 8 minutes, then the area of the park (in sq. m) is:**

- **A.** 15360
- **B.** 153600  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 30720
- **D.** 307200

**Explanation:** Perimeter = Distance covered in 8 min. = 12000 x 8 m = 1600 m. 60 Let length = 3 x metres and breadth = 2 x metres. Then, 2(3 x + 2 x ) = 1600 or x = 160. Length = 480 m and Breadth = 320 m. Area = (480 x 320) m 2 = 153600 m 2 .

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/)*

---

**Q88. What is the area of the given rectangle? I. Perimeter of the rectangle is 60 cm. II. Breadth of the rectangle is 12 cm. III. Sum of two adjacent sides is 30 cm.**

- **A.** I only  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II only
- **C.** I and II only
- **D.** II and III only

**Explanation:** From I and II, we can find the length and breadth of the rectangle and therefore the area can be obtained. So, III is redundant. Also, from II and III, we can find the length and breadth and therefore the area can be obtained. So, I is redundant. Correct answer is "II and either I or III".

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/057001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/057001)*

---

**Q89. A rectangular park 60 m long and 40 m wide has two concrete crossroads running in the middle of the park and rest of the park has been used as a lawn. If the area of the lawn is 2109 sq. m, then what is the width of the road?**

- **A.** 2.91 m
- **B.** 3 m  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 5.82 m
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Area of the park = (60 x 40) m 2 = 2400 m 2 . Area of the lawn = 2109 m 2 . Area of the crossroads = (2400 - 2109) m 2 = 291 m 2 . Let the width of the road be x metres. Then, 60 x + 40 x - x 2 = 291 x 2 - 100 x + 291 = 0 ( x - 97)( x - 3) = 0 x = 3. Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/R3CtrAKGxkc

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/)*

---

**Q90. The diagonal of a rectangle is 41 cm and its area is 20 sq. cm. The perimeter of the rectangle must be:**

- **A.** 9 cm
- **B.** 18 cm  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 20 cm
- **D.** 41 cm

**Explanation:** l 2 + b 2 = 41 . Also, lb = 20. ( l + b ) 2 = ( l 2 + b 2 ) + 2 lb = 41 + 40 = 81 ( l + b ) = 9. Perimeter = 2( l + b ) = 18 cm.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054002)*

---

**Q91. What is the area of rectangular field? I. The perimeter of the field is 110 metres. II. The length is 5 metres more than the width. III. The ratio between length and width is 6 : 5 respectively.**

- **A.** I and II only
- **B.** Any two of the three  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** All I, II and III
- **D.** I, and either II or III only

**Explanation:** I. 2( l + b ) = 110 l + b = 55. II. l = ( b + 5) l - b = 5. III. l = 6 5 l - 6 b = 0. b 5 These are three equations in l and b . We may solve them pairwise. Any two of the three will give the answer. Correct answer is (B).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/056001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/056001)*

**Q92. 50 men took a dip in a water tank 40 m long and 20 m broad on a religious day. If the average displacement of water by a man is 4 m 3 , then the rise in the water level in the tank will be:**

- **A.** 20 cm
- **B.** 25 cm  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 35 cm
- **D.** 50 cm

**Explanation:** Total volume of water displaced = (4 x 50) m 3 = 200 m 3 . Rise in water level = 200 m 0.25 m = 25 cm. 40 x 20

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002)*

**Q93. The length of a rectangular plot is 20 metres more than its breadth. If the cost of fencing the plot @ 26.50 per metre is Rs. 5300, what is the length of the plot in metres?**

- **A.** 40  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 50
- **C.** 120
- **D.** Data inadequate

**Explanation:** Let breadth = x metres. Then, length = ( x + 20) metres. Perimeter = 5300 m = 200 m. 26.50 2[( x + 20) + x ] = 200 2 x + 20 = 100 2 x = 80 x = 40. Hence, length = x + 20 = 60 m.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054003)*

**Q94. A large cube is formed from the material obtained by melting three smaller cubes of 3, 4 and 5 cm side. What is the ratio of the total surface areas of the smaller cubes and the large cube?**

- **A.** 2 : 1
- **B.** 3 : 2
- **C.** 25 : 18  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 27 : 20

**Explanation:** Volume of the large cube = (3 3 + 4 3 + 5 3 ) = 216 cm 3 . Let the edge of the large cube be a . So, a 3 = 216 a = 6 cm. Required ratio = 6 x (3 2 + 4 2 + 5 2 ) = 50 = 25 : 18. 6 x 6 2 36

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058003)*

**Q95. The difference between the length and breadth of a rectangle is 23 m. If its perimeter is 206 m, then its area is:**

- **A.** 1520 m 2
- **B.** 2420 m 2
- **C.** 2480 m 2
- **D.** 2520 m 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** We have: ( l - b ) = 23 and 2( l + b ) = 206 or ( l + b ) = 103. Solving the two equations, we get: l = 63 and b = 40. Area = ( l x b ) = (63 x 40) m 2 = 2520 m 2 .

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054003)*

**Q96. A boat having a length 3 m and breadth 2 m is floating on a lake. The boat sinks by 1 cm when a man gets on it. The mass of the man is:**

- **A.** 12 kg
- **B.** 60 kg  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 72 kg
- **D.** 96 kg

**Explanation:** Volume of water displaced = (3 x 2 x 0.01) m 3 = 0.06 m 3 . Mass of man = Volume of water displaced x Density of water = (0.06 x 1000) kg = 60 kg.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002)*

**Q97. A rectangular park 60 m long and 40 m wide has two concrete crossroads running in the middle of the park and rest of the park has been used as a lawn. If the area of the lawn is 2109 sq. m, then what is the width of the road?**

- **A.** 2.91 m
- **B.** 3 m  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 5.82 m
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Area of the park = (60 x 40) m 2 = 2400 m 2 . Area of the lawn = 2109 m 2 . Area of the crossroads = (2400 - 2109) m 2 = 291 m 2 . Let the width of the road be x metres. Then, 60 x + 40 x - x 2 = 291 x 2 - 100 x + 291 = 0 ( x - 97)( x - 3) = 0 x = 3. Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/R3CtrAKGxkc

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054001)*

**Q98. The percentage increase in the area of a rectangle, if each of its sides is increased by 20% is:**

- **A.** 40%
- **B.** 42%
- **C.** 44%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 46%

**Explanation:** Let original length = x metres and original breadth = y metres. Original area = ( xy ) m 2 . New length = 120 x m = 6 x m. 100 5 New breadth = 120 y m = 6 y m. 100 5 New Area = 6 x x 6 y m 2 = 36 xy m 2 . 5 5 25 The difference between the original area = xy and new-area 36/25 xy is = (36/25)xy - xy = xy(36/25 - 1) = xy(11/25) or (11/25)xy Increase % = 11 xy x 1 x 100 % = 44%. 25 xy Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/I3jLjLPn1W4

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054001)*

**Q99. The ratio between the length and the breadth of a rectangular park is 3 : 2. If a man cycling along the boundary of the park at the speed of 12 km/hr completes one round in 8 minutes, then the area of the park (in sq. m) is:**

- **A.** 15360
- **B.** 153600  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 30720
- **D.** 307200

**Explanation:** Perimeter = Distance covered in 8 min. = 12000 x 8 m = 1600 m. 60 Let length = 3 x metres and breadth = 2 x metres. Then, 2(3 x + 2 x ) = 1600 or x = 160. Length = 480 m and Breadth = 320 m. Area = (480 x 320) m 2 = 153600 m 2 .

**Q101. What is the total surface area of a right circular cone of height 14 cm and base radius 7 cm?**

- **A.** 344.35 cm 2
- **B.** 462 cm 2
- **C.** 498.35 cm 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** h = 14 cm, r = 7 cm. So, l = (7) 2 + (14) 2 = 245 = 7 5 cm. Total surface area = rl + r 2 = 22 x 7 x 7 5 + 22 x 7 x 7 cm 2 7 7 = [154( 5 + 1)] cm 2 = (154 x 3.236) cm 2 = 498.35 cm 2 .

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058003)*

**Q102. What is the volume of 32 metre high cylindrical tank? I. The area of its base is 154 m 2 . II. The diameter of the base is 14 m.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Given, height = 32 m. I gives, area of the base = 154 m 2 . Volume = (Area of the base x Height) = (154 x 32) m 3 . Thus, I alone gives the answer. II gives, radius of the base = 7 m. Volume = r 2 h = 22 x 7 x 7 x 32 m 3 = 4928 m 3 . 7 Thus, II alone gives the answer. Correct answer is (C).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001)*

**Q103. The ratio between the perimeter and the breadth of a rectangle is 5 : 1. If the area of the rectangle is 216 sq. cm, what is the length of the rectangle?**

- **A.** 16 cm
- **B.** 18 cm  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 24 cm
- **D.** Data inadequate

**Explanation:** 2( l + b ) = 5 b 1 2 l + 2 b = 5 b 3 b = 2 l b = 2 l 3 Then, Area = 216 cm 2 l x b = 216 l x 2 l = 216 3 l 2 = 324 l = 18 cm.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/)*

- **C.** 68
- **D.** 88  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Q109. What is the volume of a cube? I. The area of each face of the cube is 64 square metres. II. The length of one side of the cube is 8 metres.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Let each edge be a metres. Then, I. a 2 = 64 a = 8 m Volume = (8 x 8 x 8) m 3 = 512 m 3 . Thus, I alone gives the answer. II. a = 8 m Volume = (8 x 8 x 8) m 3 = 512 m 3 . Thus, II alone gives the answer. Correct answer is (C).

**Q112. What will be the cost of painting the inner walls of a room if the rate of painting is Rs. 20 per square foot? I. Circumference of the floor is 44 feet. II. The height of the wall of the room is 12 feet.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** I gives, 2 R = 44. II gives, H = 12. A = 2 RH = (44 x 12). Cost of painting = Rs. (44 x 12 x 20). Thus, I and II together give the answer. Correct answer is (E).

**Q113. What is the capacity of the cylindrical tank? I. The area of the base is 61,600 sq. cm. II. The height of the tank is 1.5 times the radius. III. The circumference of base is 880 cm.**

- **A.** Only I and II  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Only II and III
- **C.** Only I and III
- **D.** Any two of the three

**Explanation:** Capacity = r 2 h . I gives, r 2 = 61600. This gives r . II gives, h = 1.5 r . Thus, I and II give the answer. Again, III gives 2 r = 880. This gives r . So, II and III also give the answer. Correct answer is (E).

**Q116. What is the area of a right-angled triangle? I. The perimeter of the triangle is 30 cm. II. The ratio between the base and the height of the triangle is 5 : 12. III. The area of the triangle is equal to the area of a rectangle of length 10 cm.**

- **A.** I and II only  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II and III only
- **C.** I and III only
- **D.** III, and either I or II only

**Explanation:** From II, base : height = 5 : 12. Let base = 5 x and height = 12 x . Then, hypotenuse = (5 x ) 2 + (12 x ) 2 = 13 x . From I, perimeter of the triangle = 30 cm. 5 x + 12 x + 13 x = 30 x = 1. So, base = 5 x = 5 cm, height = 12 x = 12 cm. Area = 1 x 5 x 12 cm 2 = 30 cm 2 . 2 Thus, I and II together give the answer. Clearly III is redundant, since the breadth of the rectangle is not given. Correct answer is (A).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/056001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/056001)*

---

**Q117. Is a given rectangular block, a cube? I. At least 2 faces of the rectangular block are squares. II. The volume of the block is 64.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** I gives, any two of l , b , h are equal. II gives, lbh = 64. From I and II, the values of l, b, h may be (1 ,1 , 64), (2 ,2 ,16), (4, 4, 4). Thus, the block may be a cube or cuboid. Correct answer is (D).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001)*

**Q118. A hollow iron pipe is 21 cm long and its external diameter is 8 cm. If the thickness of the pipe is 1 cm and iron weighs 8 g/cm 3 , then the weight of the pipe is:**

- **A.** 3.6 kg
- **B.** 3.696 kg  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 36 kg
- **D.** 36.9 kg

**Explanation:** External radius = 4 cm, Internal radius = 3 cm. Volume of iron = 22 x [(4) 2 - (3) 2 ] x 21 cm 3 7 = 22 x 7 x 1 x 21 cm 3 7 = 462 cm 3 . Weight of iron = (462 x 8) gm = 3696 gm = 3.696 kg.

**Q121. 66 cubic centimetres of silver is drawn into a wire 1 mm in diameter. The length of the wire in metres will be:**

- **C.** 168
- **D.** 336

**Q123. A cistern of capacity 8000 litres measures externally 3.3 m by 2.6 m by 1.1 m and its walls are 5 cm thick. The thickness of the bottom is:**

- **A.** 90 cm
- **B.** 1 dm  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 1 m
- **D.** 1.1 cm

**Explanation:** Let the thickness of the bottom be x cm. Then, [(330 - 10) x (260 - 10) x (110 - x )] = 8000 x 1000 320 x 250 x (110 - x ) = 8000 x 1000 (110 - x ) = 8000 x 1000 = 100 320 x 250 x = 10 cm = 1 dm.

**Q124. An error 2% in excess is made while measuring the side of a square. The percentage of error in the calculated area of the square is:**

- **A.** 2%
- **B.** 2.02%
- **C.** 4%
- **D.** 4.04%  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** 100 cm is read as 102 cm. A 1 = (100 x 100) cm 2 and A 2 (102 x 102) cm 2 . (A 2 - A 1 ) = [(102) 2 - (100) 2 ] = (102 + 100) x (102 - 100) = 404 cm 2 . Percentage error = 404 x 100 % = 4.04% 100 x 100

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054001)*

**Q125. A man walked diagonally across a square lot. Approximately, what was the percent saved by not walking along the edges?**

- **A.** 20
- **B.** 24
- **C.** 30  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 33

**Explanation:** Let the side of the square(ABCD) be x metres. Then, AB + BC = 2 x metres. AC = 2 x = (1.41 x ) m. Saving on 2 x metres = (0.59 x ) m. Saving % = 0.59 x x 100 % = 30% (approx.) 2 x

**Q126. The area of playground is 1600 m 2 . What is the perimeter? I. It is a perfect square playground. II. It costs Rs. 3200 to put a fence around the playground at the rate of Rs. 20 per metre.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Area = 1600 m 2 . I. Side = 1600 m = 40 m. So, perimeter = (40 x 4) m = 160 m. I alone gives the answer. II. Perimeter = Total cost = 3200 m = 160 m. Cost per metre 20 II alone gives the answer. Correct answer is (C).

**Q129. What is the height of the triangle? I. The area of the triangle is 20 times its base. II. The perimeter of the triangle is equal to the perimeter of a square of side 10 cm.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** I. A = 20 x B 1 x B x H = 20 x B H = 40. 2 I alone gives the answer. II gives, perimeter of the triangle = 40 cm. This does not give the height of the triangle. Correct answer is (A).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/055001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/055001)*

---

**Q130. A tank is 25 m long, 12 m wide and 6 m deep. The cost of plastering its walls and bottom at 75 paise per sq. m, is:**

- **A.** Rs. 456
- **B.** Rs. 458
- **C.** Rs. 558  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 568

**Explanation:** Area to be plastered = [2( l + b ) x h ] + ( l x b ) = {[2(25 + 12) x 6] + (25 x 12)} m 2 = (444 + 300) m 2 = 744 m 2 . Cost of plastering = Rs. 744 x 75 = Rs. 558. 100

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/054003)*

---

**Q131. What is the capacity of a cylindrical tank? I. Radius of the base is half of its height which is 28 metres. II. Area of the base is 616 sq. metres and its height is 28 metres.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** I gives, h = 28 m and r = 14. Capacity = r 2 h , which can be obtained. Thus, I alone gives the answer. II gives, r 2 = 616 m 2 and h = 28 m. Capacity = ( r 2 x h ) = (616 x 28) m 3 . Thus, II alone gives the answer. Correct answer is (C).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/059001)*

---

**Q132. The slant height of a right circular cone is 10 m and its height is 8 m. Find the area of its curved surface.**

- **A.** 30 m 2
- **B.** 40 m 2
- **C.** 60 m 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 80 m 2

**Explanation:** l = 10 m, h = 8 m. So, r = l 2 - h 2 = (10) 2 - 8 2 = 6 m. Curved surface area = rl = ( x 6 x 10) m 2 = 60 m 2 .

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/volume-and-surface-area/058002)*

---

**Q133. What is the cost painting the two adjacent walls of a hall at Rs. 5 per m 2 which has no windows or doors? I. The area of the hall is 24 sq. m. II. The breadth, length and height of the hall are in the ratio of 4 : 6 : 5 respectively. III. Area of one wall is 30 sq. m.**

- **A.** I only
- **B.** II only
- **C.** III only  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Either I or III

**Explanation:** From II, let l = 4 x , b = 6 x and h = 5 x . Then, area of the hall = (24 x 2 ) m 2 . From I. Area of the hall = 24 m 2 . From II and I, we get 24 x 2 = 24 x = 1. l = 4 m, b = 6 and h = 5 m. Thus, area of two adjacent walls = [( l x h ) + ( b x h )] m 2 can be found out and so the cost of painting two adjacent walls may be found out. Thus, III is redundant. Correct answer is (C).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/057001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/area/057001)*

---

## Numerics: LCM & HCF

**Q134. The greatest number which on dividing 1657 and 2037 leaves remainders 6 and 5 respectively, is:**

- **A.** 123
- **B.** 127  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 235
- **D.** 305

**Explanation:** Required number = H.C.F. of (1657 - 6) and (2037 - 5) = H.C.F. of 1651 and 2032 = 127.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006)*

---

**Q135. The L.C.M. of two numbers is 48. The numbers are in the ratio 2 : 3. Then sum of the number is:**

- **A.** 28
- **B.** 32
- **C.** 40  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 64

**Explanation:** Let the numbers be 2 x and 3 x . Then, their L.C.M. = 6 x . So, 6 x = 48 or x = 8. The numbers are 16 and 24. Hence, required sum = (16 + 24) = 40.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006)*

---

**Q136. Three numbers which are co-prime to each other are such that the product of the first two is 551 and that of the last two is 1073. The sum of the three numbers is:**

- **A.** 75
- **B.** 81
- **C.** 85  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 89

**Explanation:** Since the numbers are co-prime, they contain only 1 as the common factor. Also, the given two products have the middle number in common. So, middle number = H.C.F. of 551 and 1073 = 29; First number = 551 = 19; Third number = 1073 = 37. 29 29 Required sum = (19 + 29 + 37) = 85.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002005](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002005)*

---

**Q137. Three number are in the ratio of 3 : 4 : 5 and their L.C.M. is 2400. Their H.C.F. is:**

- **A.** 40  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 80
- **C.** 120
- **D.** 200

**Explanation:** Let the numbers be 3 x , 4 x and 5 x . Then, their L.C.M. = 60 x . So, 60 x = 2400 or x = 40. The numbers are (3 x 40), (4 x 40) and (5 x 40). Hence, required H.C.F. = 40.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002002)*

---

**Q138. If the sum of two numbers is 55 and the H.C.F. and L.C.M. of these numbers are 5 and 120 respectively, then the sum of the reciprocals of the numbers is equal to:**

- **A.** 55 601
- **B.** 601 55
- **C.** 11 120  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 120 11

**Explanation:** Let the numbers be a and b . Then, a + b = 55 and ab = 5 x 120 = 600. The required sum = 1 + 1 = a + b = 55 = 11 a b ab 600 120

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006)*

---

**Q139. Let N be the greatest number that will divide 1305, 4665 and 6905, leaving the same remainder in each case. Then sum of the digits in N is:**

- **A.** 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 5
- **C.** 6
- **D.** 8

**Explanation:** N = H.C.F. of (4665 - 1305), (6905 - 4665) and (6905 - 1305) = H.C.F. of 3360, 2240 and 5600 = 1120. Sum of digits in N = ( 1 + 1 + 2 + 0 ) = 4

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002001)*

**Q140. Which of the following fraction is the largest ?**

- **A.** 7 8  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 13 16
- **C.** 31 40
- **D.** 63 80

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 8, 16, 40 and 80 = 80. 7 = 70 ; 13 = 65 ; 31 = 62 8 80 16 80 40 80 Since, 70 > 65 > 63 > 62 , so 7 > 13 > 63 > 31 80 80 80 80 8 16 80 40 So, 7 is the largest. 8

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002005](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002005)*

- **B.** 2 x 2 x 2 x 3 x 7
- **C.** 3 x 3 x 3 x 3 x 7
- **D.** 2 x 3 x 3 x 3 x 7

**Explanation:** Clearly, 252 = 2 x 2 x 3 x 3 x 7.

- **A.** 4
- **B.** 6
- **C.** 12  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 18

**Q143. Which of the following has the most number of divisors?**

- **A.** 99
- **B.** 101
- **C.** 176  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 182

**Explanation:** 99 = 1 x 3 x 3 x 11 101 = 1 x 101 176 = 1 x 2 x 2 x 2 x 2 x 11 182 = 1 x 2 x 7 x 13 So, divisors of 99 are 1, 3, 9, 11, 33, .99 Divisors of 101 are 1 and 101 Divisors of 176 are 1, 2, 4, 8, 11, 16, 22, 44, 88 and 176 Divisors of 182 are 1, 2, 7, 13, 14, 26, 91 and 182. Hence, 176 has the most number of divisors.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002006)*

**Q144. The product of two numbers is 2028 and their H.C.F. is 13. The number of such pairs is:**

- **A.** 1
- **B.** 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 3
- **D.** 4

**Explanation:** Let the numbers 13 a and 13 b . Then, 13 a x 13 b = 2028 ab = 12. Now, the co-primes with product 12 are (1, 12) and (3, 4). [Note: Two integers a and b are said to be coprime or relatively prime if they have no common positive factor other than 1 or, equivalently, if their greatest common divisor is 1 ] So, the required numbers are (13 x 1, 13 x 12) and (13 x 3, 13 x 4). Clearly, there are 2 such pairs.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002002)*

- **A.** 276
- **B.** 299

**Q148. The least number which when divided by 5, 6 , 7 and 8 leaves a remainder 3, but when divided by 9 leaves no remainder, is:**

- **A.** 1677
- **B.** 1683  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 2523
- **D.** 3363

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 5, 6, 7, 8 = 840. Required number is of the form 840 k + 3 Least value of k for which (840 k + 3) is divisible by 9 is k = 2. Required number = (840 x 2 + 3) = 1683.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002003)*

**Q149. The least number which should be added to 2497 so that the sum is exactly divisible by 5, 6, 4 and 3 is:**

- **A.** 3
- **B.** 13
- **C.** 23  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 33

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 5, 6, 4 and 3 = 60. On dividing 2497 by 60, the remainder is 37. Number to be added = (60 - 37) = 23.

**Q151. The product of two numbers is 4107. If the H.C.F. of these numbers is 37, then the greater number is:**

- **A.** 101
- **B.** 107
- **C.** 111  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 185

**Explanation:** Let the numbers be 37 a and 37 b . Then, 37 a x 37 b = 4107 ab = 3. Now, co-primes with product 3 are (1, 3). So, the required numbers are (37 x 1, 37 x 3) i.e., (37, 111). Greater number = 111.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002002)*

**Q152. The greatest number of four digits which is divisible by 15, 25, 40 and 75 is:**

- **A.** 9000
- **B.** 9400
- **C.** 9600  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 9800

**Explanation:** Greatest number of 4-digits is 9999. L.C.M. of 15, 25, 40 and 75 is 600. On dividing 9999 by 600, the remainder is 399. Required number (9999 - 399) = 9600.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/problems-on-hcf-and-lcm/002001)*

- **B.** 10
- **C.** 15
- **D.** 16  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 2, 4, 6, 8, 10, 12 is 120. So, the bells will toll together after every 120 seconds(2 minutes). In 30 minutes, they will toll together 30 + 1 = 16 times. 2

**Q160. A, B and C start at the same time in the same direction to run around a circular stadium. A completes a round in 252 seconds, B in 308 seconds and c in 198 seconds, all starting at the same point. After what time will they again at the starting point ?**

- **A.** 26 minutes and 18 seconds
- **B.** 42 minutes and 36 seconds
- **C.** 45 minutes
- **D.** 46 minutes and 12 seconds  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 252, 308 and 198 = 2772. So, A, B and C will again meet at the starting point in 2772 sec. i.e., 46 min. 12 sec.

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 6, 9, 15 and 18 is 90. Let required number be 90 k + 4, which is multiple of 7. Least value of k for which (90 k + 4) is divisible by 7 is k = 4. Required number = (90 x 4) + 4 = 364.

## Numerics: Logs and Exponents

**Q169. Which of the following statements is not correct?**

- **A.** log 10 10 = 1
- **B.** log (2 + 3) = log (2 x 3)  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** log 10 1 = 0
- **D.** log (1 + 2 + 3) = log 1 + log 2 + log 3

**Explanation:** (a) Since log a a = 1, so log 10 10 = 1. (b) log (2 + 3) = log 5 and log (2 x 3) = log 6 = log 2 + log 3 log (2 + 3) log (2 x 3) (c) Since log a 1 = 0, so log 10 1 = 0. (d) log (1 + 2 + 3) = log 6 = log (1 x 2 x 3) = log 1 + log 2 + log 3. So, (b) is incorrect.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/053001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/053001)*

---

**Q170. If log 10 2 = 0.3010, the value of log 10 80 is:**

- **A.** 1.6020
- **B.** 1.9030  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 3.9030
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** log 10 80 = log 10 (8 x 10) = log 10 8 + log 10 10 = log 10 (2 3 ) + 1 = 3 log 10 2 + 1 = (3 x 0.3010) + 1 = 1.9030.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/053002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/053002)*

---

**Q171. If log 10 7 = a , then log 10 1 is equal to: 70**

- **A.** - (1 + a )  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** (1 + a ) -1
- **C.** a 10
- **D.** 1 10 a

**Explanation:** log 10 1 70 = log 10 1 - log 10 70 = - log 10 (7 x 10) = - (log 10 7 + log 10 10) = - ( a + 1).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/053002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/053002)*

**Q172. The value of 1 + 1 + 1 is: log 3 60 log 4 60 log 5 60**

- **A.** 0
- **B.** 1  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 5
- **D.** 60

**Explanation:** Given expression = log 60 3 + log 60 4 + log 60 5 = log 60 (3 x 4 x 5) = log 60 60 = 1.

- **B.** log (2 + 3) = log (2 x 3)  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** log 10 1 = 0
- **D.** log (1 + 2 + 3) = log 1 + log 2 + log 3

**Explanation:** (a) Since log a a = 1, so log 10 10 = 1. (b) log (2 + 3) = log 5 and log (2 x 3) = log 6 = log 2 + log 3 log (2 + 3) log (2 x 3) (c) Since log a 1 = 0, so log 10 1 = 0. (d) log (1 + 2 + 3) = log 6 = log (1 x 2 x 3) = log 1 + log 2 + log 3. So, (b) is incorrect.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/logarithm/)*

**Q187. If log 10 5 + log 10 (5 x + 1) = log 10 ( x + 5) + 1, then x is equal to:**

- **D.** 10

## Numerics: Percentage

**Q189. What percentage of numbers from 1 to 70 have 1 or 9 in the unit's digit?**

- **A.** 1
- **B.** 14
- **C.** 20  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 21

**Explanation:** Clearly, the numbers which have 1 or 9 in the unit's digit, have squares that end in the digit 1. Such numbers from 1 to 70 are 1, 9, 11, 19, 21, 29, 31, 39, 41, 49, 51, 59, 61, 69. Number of such number =14 Required percentage = 14 x 100 % = 20%. 70 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/cBamI6iRNIA

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/)*

---

**Q190. A student multiplied a number by 3 instead of 5 . 5 3 What is the percentage error in the calculation?**

- **A.** 34%
- **B.** 44%
- **C.** 54%
- **D.** 64%  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the number be x . Then, error = 5 x - 3 x = 16 x . 3 5 15 Error% = 16 x x 3 x 100 % = 64%. 15 5 x

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017002)*

---

**Q191. Rajeev buys good worth Rs. 6650. He gets a rebate of 6% on it. After getting the rebate, he pays sales tax @ 10%. Find the amount he will have to pay for the goods.**

- **A.** Rs. 6876.10  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 6999.20
- **C.** Rs. 6654
- **D.** Rs. 7000

**Explanation:** Rebate = 6% of Rs. 6650 = Rs. 6 x 6650 = Rs. 399. 100 Sales tax = 10% of Rs. (6650 - 399) = Rs. 10 x 6251 = Rs. 625.10 100 Final amount = Rs. (6251 + 625.10) = Rs. 6876.10 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/XuiggCTh3SU

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017003)*

---

**Q192. A fruit seller had some apples. He sells 40% apples and still has 420 apples. Originally, he had:**

- **A.** 588 apples
- **B.** 600 apples
- **C.** 672 apples
- **D.** 700 apples  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Suppose originally he had x apples. Then, (100 - 40)% of x = 420. 60 x x = 420 100 x = 420 x 100 = 700. 60 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/-Pv25Do3WwY

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017001)*

**Q193. Gauri went to the stationers and bought things worth Rs. 25, out of which 30 paise went on sales tax on taxable purchases. If the tax rate was 6%, then what was the cost of the tax free items?**

- **A.** Rs. 15
- **B.** Rs. 15.70
- **C.** Rs. 19.70  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 20

**Explanation:** Let the amount taxable purchases be Rs. x . Then, 6% of x = 30 100 x = 30 x 100 = 5. 100 6 Cost of tax free items = Rs. [25 - (5 + 0.30)] = Rs. 19.70

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017003)*

**Q194. Two tailors X and Y are paid a total of Rs. 550 per week by their employer. If X is paid 120 percent of the sum paid to Y, how much is Y paid per week?**

- **A.** Rs. 200
- **B.** Rs. 250  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 300
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Let the sum paid to Y per week be Rs. z . Then, z + 120% of z = 550. z + 120 z = 550 100 11 z = 550 5 z = 550 x 5 = 250. 11

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017003)*

**Q195. Two students appeared at an examination. One of them secured 9 marks more than the other and his marks was 56% of the sum of their marks. The marks obtained by them are:**

- **A.** 39, 30
- **B.** 41, 32
- **C.** 42, 33  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 43, 34

**Explanation:** Let their marks be ( x + 9) and x . Then, x + 9 = 56 ( x + 9 + x ) 100 25( x + 9) = 14(2 x + 9) 3 x = 99 x = 33 So, their marks are 42 and 33.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017001)*

**Q197. In a certain school, 20% of students are below 8 years of age. The number of students above 8 years of age is of the number of students of 8 years of age which is 48. What is the total number of students in the school?**

- **A.** 72  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 80
- **C.** 120
- **D.** 150

**Explanation:** Let the number of students be x . Then, Number of students above 8 years of age = (100 - 20)% of x = 80% of x . 80% of x = 48 + 2 of 48 3 80 x = 80 100 x = 100. Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/yPfocU6DA2M

- **A.** 4.37%
- **B.** 5%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 6%
- **D.** 8.75%

**Explanation:** Increase in 10 years = (262500 - 175000) = 87500. Increase% = 87500 x 100 % = 50%. 175000 Required average = 50 % = 5%. 10

**Q199. Two numbers A and B are such that the sum of 5% of A and 4% of B is two-third of the sum of 6% of A and 8% of B. Find the ratio of A : B.**

- **A.** 2 : 3
- **B.** 1 : 1
- **C.** 3 : 4
- **D.** 4 : 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** 5% of A + 4% of B = 2 (6% of A + 8% of B) 3 5 A + 4 B = 2 6 A + 8 B 100 100 3 100 100 1 A + 1 B = 1 A + 4 B 20 25 25 75 1 - 1 A = 4 - 1 B 20 25 75 25 1 A = 1 B 100 75 A = 100 = 4 . B 75 3 Required ratio = 4 : 3 Video Explanation: YouTube Video

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/percentage/017002)*

**Q200. If A = x % of y and B = y % of x , then which of the following is true?**

- **A.** A is smaller than B.  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** A is greater than B
- **C.** Relationship between A and B cannot be determined.
- **D.** If x is smaller than y , then A is greater than B.

**Explanation:** x % of y = x x y = y x x = y % of x 100 100 A = B.

**Q202. A batsman scored 110 runs which included 3 boundaries and 8 sixes. What percent of his total score did he make by running between the wickets?**

- **A.** 45%
- **B.** 45 5 % 11  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 54 6 % 11
- **D.** 55%

**Explanation:** Number of runs made by running = 110 - (3 x 4 + 8 x 6) = 110 - (60) = 50. Required percentage = 50 x 100 % = 45 5 % 110 11 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/X2zTnABqEHU

**Q207. In an election between two candidates, one got 55% of the total valid votes, 20% of the votes were invalid. If the total number of votes was 7500, the number of valid votes that the other candidate got, was:**

- **A.** 2700  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 2900
- **C.** 3000
- **D.** 3100

**Explanation:** Number of valid votes = 80% of 7500 = 6000. Valid votes polled by other candidate = 45% of 6000 = 45 x 6000 = 2700. 100

## Numerics: Profit and Loss

**Q209. Sam purchased 20 dozens of toys at the rate of Rs. 375 per dozen. He sold each one of them at the rate of Rs. 33. What was his percentage profit?**

- **A.** 3.5
- **B.** 4.5
- **C.** 5.6  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 6.5

**Explanation:** Cost Price of 1 toy = Rs. 375 = Rs. 31.25 12 Selling Price of 1 toy = Rs. 33 So, Gain = Rs. (33 - 31.25) = Rs. 1.75 Profit % = 1.75 x 100 % = 28 % = 5.6% 31.25 5 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/MhswuvDVWzo

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018002)*

---

**Q210. In a certain store, the profit is 320% of the cost. If the cost increases by 25% but the selling price remains constant, approximately what percentage of the selling price is the profit?**

- **A.** 30%
- **B.** 70%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 100%
- **D.** 250%

**Explanation:** Let C.P.= Rs. 100. Then, Profit = Rs. 320, S.P. = Rs. 420. New C.P. = 125% of Rs. 100 = Rs. 125 New S.P. = Rs. 420. Profit = Rs. (420 - 125) = Rs. 295. Required percentage = 295 x 100 % = 1475 % = 70% (approximately). 420 21 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/bQA8SB8ycbw

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/)*

---

**Q211. A shopkeeper sells some toys at Rs. 250 each. What percent profit does he make? To find the answer, which of the following information given in Statements I and II is/are necessary? I. Number of toys sold. II. Cost price of each toy.**

- **A.** Only I is necessary
- **B.** Only II is necessary  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Both I and II are necessary
- **D.** Either I or II ins necessary

**Explanation:** S.P. = Rs. 250 each. To find gain percent, we must know the C.P. of each. Correct answer is (B).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/019001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/019001)*

---

**Q212. When a plot is sold for Rs. 18,700, the owner loses 15%. At what price must that plot be sold in order to gain 15%?**

- **A.** Rs. 21,000
- **B.** Rs. 22,500
- **C.** Rs. 25,300  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 25,800

**Explanation:** 85 : 18700 = 115 : x x = 18700 x 115 = 25300. 85 Hence, S.P. = Rs. 25,300.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018003)*

---

**Q213. In a certain store, the profit is 320% of the cost. If the cost increases by 25% but the selling price remains constant, approximately what percentage of the selling price is the profit?**

- **A.** 30%
- **B.** 70%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 100%
- **D.** 250%

**Explanation:** Let C.P.= Rs. 100. Then, Profit = Rs. 320, S.P. = Rs. 420. New C.P. = 125% of Rs. 100 = Rs. 125 New S.P. = Rs. 420. Profit = Rs. (420 - 125) = Rs. 295. Required percentage = 295 x 100 % = 1475 % = 70% (approximately). 420 21 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/bQA8SB8ycbw

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018001)*

**Q214. The cost price of 20 articles is the same as the selling price of x articles. If the profit is 25%, then the value of x is:**

- **A.** 15
- **B.** 16  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 18
- **D.** 25

**Explanation:** Let C.P. of each article be Re. 1 C.P. of x articles = Rs. x . S.P. of x articles = Rs. 20. Profit = Rs. (20 - x ). 20 - x x 100 = 25 x 2000 - 100 x = 25 x 125 x = 2000 x = 16. Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/sidqvjUoZxY

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/)*

**Q215. A trader mixes 26 kg of rice at Rs. 20 per kg with 30 kg of rice of other variety at Rs. 36 per kg and sells the mixture at Rs. 30 per kg. His profit percent is:**

- **A.** No profit, no loss
- **B.** 5%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 8%
- **D.** 10%

**Explanation:** C.P. of 56 kg rice = Rs. (26 x 20 + 30 x 36) = Rs. (520 + 1080) = Rs. 1600. S.P. of 56 kg rice = Rs. (56 x 30) = Rs. 1680. Gain = 80 x 100 % = 5%. 1600

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018003)*

**Q216. A shopkeeper expects a gain of 22.5% on his cost price. If in a week, his sale was of Rs. 392, what was his profit?**

- **A.** Rs. 18.20
- **B.** Rs. 70
- **C.** Rs. 72  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 88.25

**Explanation:** C.P. = Rs. 100 x 392 = Rs. 1000 x 392 = Rs. 320 122.5 1225 Profit = Rs. (392 - 320) = Rs. 72. Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/a36nJFgh5yk

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018002)*

**Q217. By selling a product with 20% profit, how much profit was earned? I. The difference between cost and selling price is Rs. 40. II. The selling price is 120 percent of the cost price.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Gain = 20% I. Profit = (S.P.) - (C.P.) = Rs. 40. Thus, I give the answer. But, II does not give the answer. Correct answer is (A).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/020001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/020001)*

**Q218. Some articles were bought at 6 articles for Rs. 5 and sold at 5 articles for Rs. 6. Gain percent is:**

- **A.** 30%
- **B.** 33 1 % 3
- **C.** 35%
- **D.** 44%  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Suppose, number of articles bought = L.C.M. of 6 and 5 = 30. C.P. of 30 articles = Rs. 5 x 30 = Rs. 25. 6 S.P. of 30 articles = Rs. 6 x 30 = Rs. 36. 5 Gain % = 11 x 100 % = 44%. 25

**Q219. A man mixes two types of rice (X and Y) and sells the mixture at the rate of Rs. 17 per kg. Find his profit percentage. I. The rate of X is Rs. 20 per kg. II. The rate of Y is Rs. 13 per kg.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The ratio, in which X and Y are mixed, is not given. So, both I and II together cannot give the answer. Correct answer is (D).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/020001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/020001)*

**Q220. By selling an article what is the profit percent gained? I. 5% discount is given on list price. II. If discount is not given, 20% profit is gained. III. The cost price of the articles is Rs. 5000.**

- **A.** Only I and II  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Only II and III
- **C.** Only I and III
- **D.** All I, II and III

**Explanation:** I. Let the list price be Rs. x . Then, S.P. = 95% of Rs. x = Rs. x x 95 = Rs. 19 x 100 20 II. When S.P. = Rs. x and gain = 20%. Then, C.P. = Rs. 100 x x = Rs. 5 x 120 6 Gain = 19 x - 5 x = 57 x - 50 x = 7 x 20 6 60 60 Gain % = 7 x x 6 x 100 % = 14%. 60 5 x Thus, I and II only give the answer. Correct answer is (A).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/021001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/021001)*

**Q221. On selling 17 balls at Rs. 720, there is a loss equal to the cost price of 5 balls. The cost price of a ball is:**

- **A.** Rs. 45
- **B.** Rs. 50
- **C.** Rs. 55
- **D.** Rs. 60  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** (C.P. of 17 balls) - (S.P. of 17 balls) = (C.P. of 5 balls) C.P. of 12 balls = S.P. of 17 balls = Rs.720. C.P. of 1 ball = Rs. 720 = Rs. 60. 12

**Q224. The percentage profit earned by selling an article for Rs. 1920 is equal to the percentage loss incurred by selling the same article for Rs. 1280. At what price should the article be sold to make 25% profit?**

- **A.** Rs. 2000  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 2200
- **C.** Rs. 2400
- **D.** Data inadequate

**Explanation:** Let C.P. be Rs. x . Then, 1920 - x x 100 = x - 1280 x 100 x x 1920 - x = x - 1280 2 x = 3200 x = 1600 Required S.P. = 125% of Rs. 1600 = Rs. 125 x 1600 = Rs 2000. 100 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/0tTd5TwCspY

**Q225. A shopkeeper sells one transistor for Rs. 840 at a gain of 20% and another for Rs. 960 at a loss of 4%. His total gain or loss percent is:**

- **A.** 5 15 % loss 17
- **B.** 5 15 % gain 17  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 6 2 % gain 3
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** C.P. of 1 st transistor = Rs. 100 x 840 = Rs. 700. 120 C.P. of 2 nd transistor = Rs. 100 x 960 = Rs. 1000 96 So, total C.P. = Rs. (700 + 1000) = Rs. 1700. Total S.P. = Rs. (840 + 960) = Rs. 1800. Gain % = 100 x 100 % = 5 15 % 1700 17

**Q226. A vendor bought toffees at 6 for a rupee. How many for a rupee must he sell to gain 20%?**

- **A.** 3
- **B.** 4
- **C.** 5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 6

**Explanation:** C.P. of 6 toffees = Re. 1 S.P. of 6 toffees = 120% of Re. 1 = Rs. 6 5 For Rs. 6 , toffees sold = 6. 5 For Re. 1, toffees sold = 6 x 5 = 5. 6 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/7wKrnZ0LKA8

**Q227. What was the percentage of discount given? I. 23.5% profit was earned by selling an almirah for Rs. 12,350. II. If there were no discount, the earned profit would have been 30%. III. The cost price of the almirah was Rs. 10,000.**

- **A.** Only I and II  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Only II and III
- **C.** Only I and III
- **D.** Any two of the three

**Explanation:** I. S.P. = Rs. 12350, Gain = 23.5% C.P. = Rs. 100 x 12350 = Rs. 10,000. 123.5 II. M.P. = 130% of C.P. = 130% of Rs. 10,000 = Rs. 13,000. From I and II, discount = Rs. (13000 - 12350) = Rs. 650. Discount % = 650 x 100 % = 5%. 13000 Thus, I and II give the answer. II and III can not give the answer. Because we require profit percentage with discount and profit percentage without discount. So II and III are not sufficient. Since III gives C.P. = Rs. 10,000, I and III give the answer. Therefore, I and II [or] I and III give the answer. Correct answer is (E).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/021001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/021001)*

---

**Q228. Alfred buys an old scooter for Rs. 4700 and spends Rs. 800 on its repairs. If he sells the scooter for Rs. 5800, his gain percent is:**

- **A.** 4 4 % 7
- **B.** 5 5 % 11  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 10%
- **D.** 12%

**Explanation:** Cost Price (C.P.) = Rs. (4700 + 800) = Rs. 5500. Selling Price (S.P.) = Rs. 5800. Gain = (S.P.) - (C.P.) = Rs.(5800 - 5500) = Rs. 300. Gain % = 300 x 100 % = 5 5 % 5500 11

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/)*

**Q229. What is the percent profit earned by the shopkeeper on selling the articles in his shop? I. Labeled price of the articles sold was 130% of the cost price. II. Cost price of each article was Rs. 550. III. A discount of 10% on labeled price was offered.**

- **A.** Only I
- **B.** Only II
- **C.** I and III  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** All the three are required

**Explanation:** I. Let C.P. be Rs. x . Then, M.P. = 130% of x = Rs. 13 x . 10 III. S.P. = 90% of M.P. Thus, I and III give, S.P. = Rs. 90 x 13 x = Rs. 117 x 100 10 100 Gain = Rs. 117 x - x = Rs. 17 x 100 100 Thus, from I and III, gain % can be obtained. Clearly, II is redundant.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/022001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/022001)*

**Q230. If selling price is doubled, the profit triples. Find the profit percent.**

- **A.** 66 2 3
- **B.** 100  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 105 1 3
- **D.** 120

**Explanation:** Let C.P. be Rs. x and S.P. be Rs. y . Then, 3( y - x ) = (2 y - x ) y = 2 x . Profit = Rs. ( y - x ) = Rs. (2 x - x ) = Rs. x . Profit % = x x 100 % = 100% x Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/dPzF10mGsWE

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/profit-and-loss/018001)*

- **C.** 10%
- **D.** 12%

- **A.** Only I is necessary
- **B.** Only II is necessary
- **C.** Either I or II is necessary
- **D.** Both I and II are necessary  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Gain = 25% of C.P. In order to find gain, we must know the sale price of each article and the number of articles sold. Correct answer is (D).

## Numerics: Ratio and Proportion

**Q236. A and B together have Rs. 1210. If of A's amount is equal to of B's amount, how much amount does B have?**

- **A.** Rs. 460
- **B.** Rs. 484  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 550
- **D.** Rs. 664

**Explanation:** 4 A = 2 B 15 5 A = 2 x 15 B 5 4 A = 3 B 2 A = 3 B 2 A : B = 3 : 2. B's share = Rs. 1210 x 2 = Rs. 484. 5

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/)*

---

**Q237. Salaries of Ravi and Sumit are in the ratio 2 : 3. If the salary of each is increased by Rs. 4000, the new ratio becomes 40 : 57. What is Sumit's salary?**

- **A.** Rs. 17,000
- **B.** Rs. 20,000
- **C.** Rs. 25,500
- **D.** Rs. 38,000  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the original salaries of Ravi and Sumit be Rs. 2 x and Rs. 3 x respectively. Then, 2 x + 4000 = 40 3 x + 4000 57 57(2 x + 4000) = 40(3 x + 4000) 6 x = 68,000 3 x = 34,000 Sumit's present salary = (3 x + 4000) = Rs.(34000 + 4000) = Rs. 38,000.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002)*

---

**Q238. In a mixture 60 litres, the ratio of milk and water 2 : 1. If this ratio is to be 1 : 2, then the quantity of water to be further added is:**

- **A.** 20 litres
- **B.** 30 litres
- **C.** 40 litres
- **D.** 60 litres  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Quantity of milk = 60 x 2 litres = 40 litres. 3 Quantity of water in it = (60- 40) litres = 20 litres. New ratio = 1 : 2 Let quantity of water to be added further be x litres. Then, milk : water = 40 . 20 + x Now, 40 = 1 20 + x 2 20 + x = 80 x = 60. Quantity of water to be added = 60 litres.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001)*

---

**Q239. The sum of three numbers is 98. If the ratio of the first to second is 2 :3 and that of the second to the third is 5 : 8, then the second number is:**

- **A.** 20
- **B.** 30  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 48
- **D.** 58

**Explanation:** Let the three parts be A, B, C. Then, A : B = 2 : 3 and B : C = 5 : 8 = 5 x 3 : 8 x 3 = 3 : 24 5 5 5 A : B : C = 2 : 3 : 24 = 10 : 15 : 24 5 B = 98 x 15 = 30. 49

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002)*

---

- **A.** Rs. 460
- **B.** Rs. 484  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 550
- **D.** Rs. 664

**Explanation:** 4 A = 2 B 15 5 A = 2 x 15 B 5 4 A = 3 B 2 A = 3 B 2 A : B = 3 : 2. B's share = Rs. 1210 x 2 = Rs. 484. 5

**Q241. The salaries A, B, C are in the ratio 2 : 3 : 5. If the increments of 15%, 10% and 20% are allowed respectively in their salaries, then what will be new ratio of their salaries?**

- **A.** 3 : 3 : 10
- **B.** 10 : 11 : 20
- **C.** 23 : 33 : 60  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Cannot be determined

**Explanation:** Let A = 2 k , B = 3 k and C = 5 k . A's new salary = 115 of 2 k = 115 x 2 k = 23 k 100 100 10 B's new salary = 110 of 3 k = 110 x 3 k = 33 k 100 100 10 C's new salary = 120 of 5 k = 120 x 5 k = 6 k 100 100 New ratio 23 k : 33 k : 6 k = 23 : 33 : 60 10 10

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003)*

---

**Q242. Two number are in the ratio 3 : 5. If 9 is subtracted from each, the new numbers are in the ratio 12 : 23. The smaller number is:**

- **A.** 27
- **B.** 33  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 49
- **D.** 55

**Explanation:** Let the numbers be 3 x and 5 x . Then, 3 x - 9 = 12 5 x - 9 23 23(3 x - 9) = 12(5 x - 9) 9 x = 99 x = 11. The smaller number = (3 x 11) = 33.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003)*

**Q243. If Rs. 782 be divided into three parts, proportional to : : , then the first part is:**

- **A.** Rs. 182
- **B.** Rs. 190
- **C.** Rs. 196
- **D.** Rs. 204  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Given ratio = : : = 6 : 8 : 9. 1 st part = Rs. 782 x 6 = Rs. 204 23

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002)*

**Q244. Seats for Mathematics, Physics and Biology in a school are in the ratio 5 : 7 : 8. There is a proposal to increase these seats by 40%, 50% and 75% respectively. What will be the ratio of increased seats?**

- **A.** 2 : 3 : 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 6 : 7 : 8
- **C.** 6 : 8 : 9
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Originally, let the number of seats for Mathematics, Physics and Biology be 5 x , 7 x and 8 x respectively. Number of increased seats are (140% of 5 x ), (150% of 7 x ) and (175% of 8 x ). 140 x 5 x , 150 x 7 x and 175 x 8 x 100 100 100 7 x , 21 x and 14 x . 2 The required ratio = 7 x : 21 x : 14 x 2 14 x : 21 x : 28 x 2 : 3 : 4.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001)*

**Q247. If 40% of a number is equal to two-third of another number, what is the ratio of first number to the second number?**

- **A.** 2 : 5
- **B.** 3 : 7
- **C.** 5 : 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 7 : 3

**Explanation:** Let 40% of A = 2 B 3 Then, 40A = 2B 100 3 2A = 2B 5 3 A = 2 x 5 = 5 B 3 2 3 A : B = 5 : 3.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003)*

**Q248. Two numbers are respectively 20% and 50% more than a third number. The ratio of the two numbers is:**

- **A.** 2 : 5
- **B.** 3 : 5
- **C.** 4 : 5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 6 : 7

**Explanation:** Let the third number be x . Then, first number = 120% of x = 120 x = 6 x 100 5 Second number = 150% of x = 150 x = 3 x 100 2 Ratio of first two numbers = 6 x : 3 x = 12 x : 15 x = 4 : 5. 5 2

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001)*

**Q249. A sum of money is to be distributed among A, B, C, D in the proportion of 5 : 2 : 4 : 3. If C gets Rs. 1000 more than D, what is B's share?**

- **A.** Rs. 500
- **B.** Rs. 1500
- **C.** Rs. 2000  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Let the shares of A, B, C and D be Rs. 5 x , Rs. 2 x , Rs. 4 x and Rs. 3 x respectively. Then, 4 x - 3 x = 1000 x = 1000. B's share = Rs. 2 x = Rs. (2 x 1000) = Rs. 2000.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023001)*

---

**Q250. The ratio of the number of boys and girls in a college is 7 : 8. If the percentage increase in the number of boys and girls be 20% and 10% respectively, what will be the new ratio?**

- **A.** 8 : 9
- **B.** 17 : 18
- **C.** 21 : 22  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Cannot be determined

**Explanation:** Originally, let the number of boys and girls in the college be 7 x and 8 x respectively. Their increased number is (120% of 7 x ) and (110% of 8 x ). 120 x 7 x and 110 x 8 x 100 100 42 x and 44 x 5 5 The required ratio = 42 x : 44 x = 21 : 22. 5 5

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023002)*

---

**Q251. Two numbers are respectively 20% and 50% more than a third number. The ratio of the two numbers is:**

- **A.** 2 : 5
- **B.** 3 : 5
- **C.** 4 : 5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 6 : 7

**Explanation:** Let the third number be x . Then, first number = 120% of x = 120 x = 6 x 100 5 Second number = 150% of x = 150 x = 3 x 100 2 Ratio of first two numbers = 6 x : 3 x = 12 x : 15 x = 4 : 5. 5 2

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/)*

**Q252. In a bag, there are coins of 25 p, 10 p and 5 p in the ratio of 1 : 2 : 3. If there is Rs. 30 in all, how many 5 p coins are there?**

- **A.** 50
- **B.** 100
- **C.** 150  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 200

**Explanation:** Let the number of 25 p, 10 p and 5 p coins be x , 2 x , 3 x respectively. Then, sum of their values = Rs. 25 x + 10 x 2 x + 5 x 3 x = Rs. 60 x 100 100 100 100 60 x = 30 x = 30 x 100 = 50. 100 60 Hence, the number of 5 p coins = (3 x 50) = 150.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/023003)*

- **D.** 1.30

**Explanation:** ( x x 5) = (0.75 x 8) x = 6 = 1.20 5
