**Q254. A sum of money is to be distributed among A, B, C, D in the proportion of 5 : 2 : 4 : 3. If C gets Rs. 1000 more than D, what is B's share?**

- **A.** Rs. 500
- **B.** Rs. 1500
- **C.** Rs. 2000  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Let the shares of A, B, C and D be Rs. 5 x , Rs. 2 x , Rs. 4 x and Rs. 3 x respectively. Then, 4 x - 3 x = 1000 x = 1000. B's share = Rs. 2 x = Rs. (2 x 1000) = Rs. 2000.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/ratio-and-proportion/)*

## Numerics: Simple Interest & Compound Interest

**Q256. The difference between simple and compound interests compounded annually on a certain sum of money for 2 years at 4% per annum is Re. 1. The sum (in Rs.) is:**

- **A.** 625  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 630
- **C.** 640
- **D.** 650

**Explanation:** Let the sum be Rs. x . Then, C.I. = x 1 + 4 2 - x = 676 x - x = 51 x . 100 625 625 S.I. = x x 4 x 2 = 2 x . 100 25 51 x - 2 x = 1 625 25 x = 625.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001)*

---

**Q257. Mr. Gupta borrowed a sum of money on compound interest. What will be the amount to be repaid if he is repaying the entire amount at the end of 2 years? I. The rate of interest is 5 p.c.p.a. II. Simple interest fetched on the same amount in one year is Rs. 600. III. The amount borrowed is 10 times the simple interest in 2 years.**

- **A.** I only
- **B.** III only
- **C.** I or II only
- **D.** II and Either I or III only  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** I. gives, Rate = 5% p.a. II. gives, S.I. for 1 year = Rs. 600. III. gives, sum = 10 x (S.I. for 2 years). Now I, and II give the sum. For this sum, C.I. and hence amount can be obtained. Thus, III is redundant. Again, II gives S.I. for 2 years = Rs. (600 x 2) = Rs. 1200. Now, from III, Sum = Rs. (10 x 1200) = Rs . 12000. Thus, Rate = 100 x 1200 = 5% p.a. 2 x 12000 Thus, C.I. for 2 years and therefore, amount can be obtained. Thus, I is redundant. Hence, I or III redundant.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/052001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/052001)*

---

**Q258. What is the difference between the compound interests on Rs. 5000 for 1 years at 4% per annum compounded yearly and half-yearly?**

- **A.** Rs. 2.04  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 3.06
- **C.** Rs. 4.80
- **D.** Rs. 8.30

**Explanation:** C.I. when interest compounded yearly = Rs. 5000 x 1 + 4 x 1 + x 4 100 100 = Rs. 5000 x 26 x 51 25 50 = Rs. 5304. C.I. when interest is compounded half-yearly = Rs. 5000 x 1 + 2 3 100 = Rs. 5000 x 51 x 51 x 51 50 50 50 = Rs. 5306.04 Difference = Rs. (5306.04 - 5304) = Rs. 2.04

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001)*

---

**Q259. What is the difference between the compound interests on Rs. 5000 for 1 years at 4% per annum compounded yearly and half-yearly?**

- **A.** Rs. 2.04  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 3.06
- **C.** Rs. 4.80
- **D.** Rs. 8.30

**Explanation:** C.I. when interest compounded yearly = Rs. 5000 x 1 + 4 x 1 + x 4 100 100 = Rs. 5000 x 26 x 51 25 50 = Rs. 5304. C.I. when interest is compounded half-yearly = Rs. 5000 x 1 + 2 3 100 = Rs. 5000 x 51 x 51 x 51 50 50 50 = Rs. 5306.04 Difference = Rs. (5306.04 - 5304) = Rs. 2.04

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/)*

**Q260. What is the rate of compound interest? I. The principal was invested for 4 years. II. The earned interest was Rs. 1491.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let Principal = Rs. P and Rate = R% p.a. Then, Amount = Rs. P 1 + R 4 100 C.I. = P 1 + R 4 - 1 100 P 1 + R 4 - 1 = 1491. 100 Clearly, it does not give the answer. Correct answer is (D).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/050001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/050001)*

**Q261. A person borrows Rs. 5000 for 2 years at 4% p.a. simple interest. He immediately lends it to another person at 6 % p.a for 2 years. Find his gain in the transaction per year.**

- **A.** Rs. 112.50  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 125
- **C.** Rs. 225
- **D.** Rs. 167.50

**Explanation:** Gain in 2 years = Rs. 5000 x 25 x 2 - 5000 x 4 x 2 4 100 100 = Rs. (625 - 400) = Rs. 225. Gain in 1 year = Rs. 225 = Rs. 112.50 2 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/zBjcwqIcmL4

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046003)*

**Q262. There is 60% increase in an amount in 6 years at simple interest. What will be the compound interest of Rs. 12,000 after 3 years at the same rate?**

- **A.** Rs. 2160
- **B.** Rs. 3120
- **C.** Rs. 3972  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 6240

**Explanation:** Let P = Rs. 100. Then, S.I. Rs. 60 and T = 6 years. R = 100 x 60 = 10% p.a. 100 x 6 Now, P = Rs. 12000. T = 3 years and R = 10% p.a. C.I. = Rs. 12000 x 1 + 10 3 - 1 100 = Rs. 12000 x 331 1000 = 3972.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001)*

- **A.** Rs. 4462.50
- **B.** Rs. 8032.50
- **C.** Rs. 8900
- **D.** Rs. 8925  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Principal = Rs. 100 x 4016.25 9 x 5 = Rs. 401625 45 = Rs. 8925.

**Q265. If the simple interest on a sum of money for 2 years at 5% per annum is Rs. 50, what is the compound interest on the same at the same rate and for the same time?**

- **A.** Rs. 51.25  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 52
- **C.** Rs. 54.25
- **D.** Rs. 60

**Explanation:** Sum = Rs. 50 x 100 = Rs. 500. 2 x 5 Amount = Rs. 500 x 1 + 5 2 100 = Rs. 500 x 21 x 21 20 20 = Rs. 551.25 C.I. = Rs. (551.25 - 500) = Rs. 51.25

**Q266. What will be compounded amount? I. Rs. 200 was borrowed for 192 months at 6% compounded annually. II. Rs. 200 was borrowed for 16 years at 6%.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** I. Amount = Rs. 200 x 1 + 6 16 100 II. Amount = Rs. 200 x 1 + 6 16 100 Thus, I as well as II gives the answer. Correct answer is (C).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/050001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/050001)*

**Q267. What is the compound interest earned at the end of 3 years? I. Simple interest earned on that amount at the same rate and for the same period is Rs. 4500. II. The rate of interest is 10 p.c.p.a. III. Compound interest for 3 years is more than the simple interest for that period by Rs. 465.**

- **A.** I and II only
- **B.** II and III only
- **C.** I and III only
- **D.** I and Either II or III only  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** I. gives, S.I for 3 years = Rs. 4500. II. gives, Rate = 10% p.a. III. gives, (C.I.) - (S.I.) = Rs. 465. Clearly, using I and III we get C.I. = Rs. (465 + 4500). Thus, II is redundant. Also, from I and II, we get sum = 100 x 4500 = 15000. 10 x 3 Now C.I. on Rs. 15000 at 10% p.a. for 3 years may be obtained. Thus, III is redundant. Either II or III is redundant.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/052001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/052001)*

**Q268. The compound interest on Rs. 30,000 at 7% per annum is Rs. 4347. The period (in years) is:**

- **A.** 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 2 1 2
- **C.** 3
- **D.** 4

**Explanation:** Amount = Rs. (30000 + 4347) = Rs. 34347. Let the time be n years. Then, 30000 1 + 7 n = 34347 100 107 n = 34347 = 11449 = 107 2 100 30000 10000 100 n = 2 years.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001)*

**Q271. What is the rate of simple interest? I. The total interest earned was Rs. 4000. II. The sum was invested for 4 years.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** We know that, R = 100 x S.I. P x T Now, I gives, S.I. = Rs. 4000. II gives, T = 4 years. But, P is unknown. So, we cannot find R. So, given data is insufficient to get R. Correct answer is (D).

**Q273. A sum of money amounts to Rs. 9800 after 5 years and Rs. 12005 after 8 years at the same rate of simple interest. The rate of interest per annum is:**

- **A.** 5%
- **B.** 8%
- **C.** 12%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 15%

**Explanation:** S.I. for 3 years = Rs. (12005 - 9800) = Rs. 2205. S.I. for 5 years = Rs. 2205 x 5 = Rs. 3675 3 Principal = Rs. (9800 - 3675) = Rs. 6125. Hence, rate = 100 x 3675 % = 12% 6125 x 5 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/UYwiBCRN39s

**Q274. The least number of complete years in which a sum of money put out at 20% compound interest will be more than doubled is:**

- **A.** 3
- **B.** 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 5
- **D.** 6

**Explanation:** P 1 + 20 n > 2P 6 n > 2. 100 5 Now, 6 x 6 x 6 x 6 > 2. 5 5 5 5 So, n = 4 years.

**Q275. A sum of money at simple interest amounts to Rs. 815 in 3 years and to Rs. 854 in 4 years. The sum is:**

- **A.** Rs. 650
- **B.** Rs. 690
- **C.** Rs. 698  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 700

**Explanation:** S.I. for 1 year = Rs. (854 - 815) = Rs. 39. S.I. for 3 years = Rs.(39 x 3) = Rs. 117. Principal = Rs. (815 - 117) = Rs. 698.

**Q277. The effective annual rate of interest corresponding to a nominal rate of 6% per annum payable half-yearly is:**

- **A.** 6.06%
- **B.** 6.07%

- **D.** 6.09%  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Q278. What percentage of simple interest per annum did Anand pay to Deepak? I. Anand borrowed Rs. 8000 from Deepak for four years. II. Anand returned Rs. 8800 to Deepak at the end of two years and settled the loan.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Let the rate be R% p.a. I gives, P = Rs. 8000 and T = 4 years. II gives, S.I. = Rs. (8800 - 8000) = Rs. 800. R = 100 x S.I. = 100 x 800 % = 2 1 % p.a. P x T 8000 x 4 2 Thus, I and II both are needed to get the answer. Correct answer is (E).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/047001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/047001)*

**Q279. A bank offers 5% compound interest calculated on half-yearly basis. A customer deposits Rs. 1600 each on 1 st January and 1 st July of a year. At the end of the year, the amount he would have gained by way of interest is:**

- **A.** Rs. 120
- **B.** Rs. 121  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 122
- **D.** Rs. 123

**Explanation:** Amount = Rs. 1600 x 1 + 5 2 + 1600 x 1 + 5 2 x 100 2 x 100 = Rs. 1600 x 41 x 41 + 1600 x 41 40 40 40 = Rs. 1600 x 41 41 + 1 40 40 = Rs. 1600 x 41 x 81 40 x 40 = Rs. 3321. C.I. = Rs. (3321 - 3200) = Rs. 121

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/049001)*

**Q280. What is the rate of interest p.c.p.a.? I. An amount doubles itself in 5 years on simple interest. II. Difference between the compound interest and the simple interest earned on a certain amount in 2 years is Rs. 400. III. Simple interest earned per annum is Rs. 2000.**

- **A.** I only  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II and III only
- **C.** All I, II and III
- **D.** Any two of the three

**Explanation:** I. P x R x 5 = P R = 20. 100 II. P 1 + R 2 - P - P x R x 2 = 400 PR 2 = 4000000. 100 100 III. P x R x 1 = 2000 PR = 200000. 100 PR 2 = 4000000 R = 20. PR 200000 Thus I only or (II and III) give answer. Correct answer is (E).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/051001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/051001)*

**Q282. An amount of money was lent for 3 years. What will be the difference between the simple and the compound interest earned on it at the same rate? I. The rate of interest was 8 p.c.p.a. II. The total amount of simple interest was Rs. 1200.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Given: T = 3 years. I. gives: R = 8% p.a. II. gives: S.I. = Rs. 1200. Thus, P = Rs. 5000, R = 8% p.a. and T = 3 years. Difference between C.I. and S.I. may be obtained. So, the correct answer is (E).

**Q284. The simple interest on a sum of money is Rs. 50. What is the sum? I. The interest rate is 10% p.a. II. The sum earned simple interest in 10 years.**

- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Given : S.I. = Rs. 50. I gives, R = 10% p.a. II gives, T = 10 years. Sum = 100 x S.I. = Rs. 100 x 50 = Rs. 50. T x R 10 x 10 Thus, I and II together give the answer. Correct answer is (E).

**Q287. What will be the ratio of simple interest earned by certain amount at the same rate of interest for 6 years and that for 9 years?**

- **A.** 1 : 3
- **B.** 1 : 4
- **C.** 2 : 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Data inadequate

**Explanation:** Let the principal be P and rate of interest be R%. Required ratio = P x R x 6 100 = 6PR = 6 = 2 : 3. P x R x 9 100 9PR 9 Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/GaaEDwTWc6w

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046003)*

**Q288. The difference between simple and compound interests compounded annually on a certain sum of money for 2 years at 4% per annum is Re. 1. The sum (in Rs.) is:**

- **A.** 625  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 630
- **C.** 640
- **D.** 650

**Explanation:** Let the sum be Rs. x . Then, C.I. = x 1 + 4 2 - x = 676 x - x = 51 x . 100 625 625 S.I. = x x 4 x 2 = 2 x . 100 25 51 x - 2 x = 1 625 25 x = 625.

**Q289. A sum of Rs. 725 is lent in the beginning of a year at a certain rate of interest. After 8 months, a sum of Rs. 362.50 more is lent but at the rate twice the former. At the end of the year, Rs. 33.50 is earned as interest from both the loans. What was the original rate of interest?**

- **A.** 3.6%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 4.5%
- **C.** 5%
- **D.** 6%

**Explanation:** Let the original rate be R%. Then, new rate = (2R)%. Note: Here, original rate is for 1 year(s); the new rate is for only 4 months i.e. year(s). 725 x R x 1 + 362.50 x 2R x 1 = 33.50 100 100 x 3 (2175 + 725) R = 33.50 x 100 x 3 (2175 + 725) R = 10050 (2900)R = 10050 R = 10050 = 3.46 2900 Original rate = 3.46%

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046002)*

**Q291. What is the sum which earned interest? I. The total simple interest was Rs. 7000 after 7 years. II. The total of sum and simple interest was double of the sum after 5 years.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** Let the sum be Rs. x . I gives, S.I. = Rs. 7000 and T = 7 years. II gives, Sum + S.I. for 5 years = 2 x Sum Sum = S.I. for 5 years. Now, S.I. for 7 years = Rs. 7000. S.I. for 1 year = Rs. 7000 = Rs. 1000. 7 Thus, I and II both are needed to get the answer. Correct answer is (E).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/047001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/047001)*

**Q292. The compound interest on a certain sum for 2 years at 10% per annum is Rs. 525. The simple interest on the same sum for double the time at half the rate percent per annum is:**

- **A.** Rs. 400
- **B.** Rs. 500  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 600
- **D.** Rs. 800

**Explanation:** Let the sum be Rs. P. Then, P 1 + 10 2 - P = 525 100 P 11 2 - 1 = 525 10 P = 525 x 100 = 2500. 21 Sum = Rs . 2500. So, S.I. = Rs. 2500 x 5 x 4 = Rs. 500 100

**Q293. Mr. Thomas invested an amount of Rs. 13,900 divided in two different schemes A and B at the simple interest rate of 14% p.a. and 11% p.a. respectively. If the total amount of simple interest earned in 2 years be Rs. 3508, what was the amount invested in Scheme B?**

- **A.** Rs. 6400  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** Rs. 6500
- **C.** Rs. 7200
- **D.** Rs. 7500

**Explanation:** Let the sum invested in Scheme A be Rs. x and that in Scheme B be Rs. (13900 - x ). Then, x x 14 x 2 + (13900 - x ) x 11 x 2 = 3508 100 100 28 x - 22 x = 350800 - (13900 x 22) 6 x = 45000 x = 7500. So, sum invested in Scheme B = Rs. (13900 - 7500) = Rs. 6400. Video Explanation: https://youtu.be/Xi4kU9y6ppk

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046001)*

- **D.** I and III only

**Q299. A bank offers 5% compound interest calculated on half-yearly basis. A customer deposits Rs. 1600 each on 1 st January and 1 st July of a year. At the end of the year, the amount he would have gained by way of interest is:**

- **A.** Rs. 120
- **B.** Rs. 121  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 122
- **D.** Rs. 123

**Explanation:** Amount = Rs. 1600 x 1 + 5 2 + 1600 x 1 + 5 2 x 100 2 x 100 = Rs. 1600 x 41 x 41 + 1600 x 41 40 40 40 = Rs. 1600 x 41 41 + 1 40 40 = Rs. 1600 x 41 x 81 40 x 40 = Rs. 3321. C.I. = Rs. (3321 - 3200) = Rs. 121

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/compound-interest/)*

**Q300. An automobile financier claims to be lending money at simple interest, but he includes the interest every six months for calculating the principal. If he is charging an interest of 10%, the effective rate of interest becomes:**

- **A.** 10%
- **B.** 10.25%  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 10.5%
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Let the sum be Rs. 100. Then, S.I. for first 6 months = Rs. 100 x 10 x 1 = Rs. 5 100 x 2 S.I. for last 6 months = Rs. 105 x 10 x 1 = Rs. 5.25 100 x 2 So, amount at the end of 1 year = Rs. (100 + 5 + 5.25) = Rs. 110.25 Effective rate = (110.25 - 100) = 10.25%

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simple-interest/046002)*

- **A.** 3.6

- **C.** 18
- **D.** Cannot be determined

**Q302. There is 60% increase in an amount in 6 years at simple interest. What will be the compound interest of Rs. 12,000 after 3 years at the same rate?**

- **A.** Rs. 2160
- **B.** Rs. 3120
- **C.** Rs. 3972  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 6240

**Explanation:** Let P = Rs. 100. Then, S.I. Rs. 60 and T = 6 years. R = 100 x 60 = 10% p.a. 100 x 6 Now, P = Rs. 12000. T = 3 years and R = 10% p.a. C.I. = Rs. 12000 x 1 + 10 3 - 1 100 = Rs. 12000 x 331 1000 = 3972.

- **D.** Cannot be determined

**Q305. A lent Rs. 5000 to B for 2 years and Rs. 3000 to C for 4 years on simple interest at the same rate of interest and received Rs. 2200 in all from both of them as interest. The rate of interest per annum is:**

- **A.** 5%
- **B.** 7%
- **C.** 7 1 % 8
- **D.** 10%  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Q306. A sum of money at simple interest amounts to Rs. 815 in 3 years and to Rs. 854 in 4 years. The sum is:**

- **A.** Rs. 650
- **B.** Rs. 690
- **C.** Rs. 698  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 700

**Explanation:** S.I. for 1 year = Rs. (854 - 815) = Rs. 39. S.I. for 3 years = Rs.(39 x 3) = Rs. 117. Principal = Rs. (815 - 117) = Rs. 698.

## Numerics: Simplification

**Q307. If a - b = 3 and a 2 + b 2 = 29, find the value of ab.**

- **A.** 10  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 12
- **C.** 15
- **D.** 18

**Explanation:** 2 ab = ( a 2 + b 2 ) - ( a - b ) 2 = 29 - 9 = 20 ab = 10.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001)*

---

**Q308. A man has some hens and cows. If the number of heads be 48 and the number of feet equals 140, then the number of hens will be:**

- **A.** 22
- **B.** 23
- **C.** 24
- **D.** 26  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the number of hens be x and the number of cows be y . Then, x + y = 48 .... (i) and 2 x + 4 y = 140 x + 2 y = 70 .... (ii) Solving (i) and (ii) we get: x = 26, y = 22. The required answer = 26.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003)*

---

**Q309. In a regular week, there are 5 working days and for each day, the working hours are 8. A man gets Rs. 2.40 per hour for regular work and Rs. 3.20 per hours for overtime. If he earns Rs. 432 in 4 weeks, then how many hours does he work for ?**

- **A.** 160
- **B.** 175  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 180
- **D.** 195

**Explanation:** Suppose the man works overtime for x hours. Now, working hours in 4 weeks = (5 x 8 x 4) = 160. 160 x 2.40 + x x 3.20 = 432 3.20 x = 432 - 384 = 48 x = 15. Hence, total hours of work = (160 + 15) = 175.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003)*

---

**Q310. A man has Rs.480 in the denominations of one-rupee notes, five-rupee notes and ten-rupee notes. The number of notes of each denomination is equal. What is the total number of notes that he has ?**

- **A.** 45
- **B.** 60
- **C.** 75
- **D.** 90  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let number of notes of each denomination be x . Then x + 5 x + 10 x = 480 16 x = 480 x = 30. Hence, total number of notes = 3 x = 90.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001)*

---

**Q311. The price of 2 sarees and 4 shirts is Rs. 1600. With the same money one can buy 1 saree and 6 shirts. If one wants to buy 12 shirts, how much shall he have to pay ?**

- **A.** Rs. 1200
- **B.** Rs. 2400  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 4800
- **D.** Cannot be determined

**Explanation:** Let the price of a saree and a shirt be Rs. x and Rs. y respectively. Then, 2 x + 4 y = 1600 .... (i) and x + 6 y = 1600 .... (ii) Divide equation (i) by 2, we get the below equation. => x + 2y = 800. --- (iii) Now subtract (iii) from (ii) x + 6y = 1600 (-) x + 2y = 800 ---------------- 4y = 800 ---------------- Therefore, y = 200. Now apply value of y in (iii) => x + 2 x 200 = 800 => x + 400 = 800 Therefore x = 400 Solving (i) and (ii) we get x = 400, y = 200. Cost of 12 shirts = Rs. (12 x 200) = Rs. 2400.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001)*

---

**Q312. Eight people are planning to share equally the cost of a rental car. If one person withdraws from the arrangement and the others share equally the entire cost of the car, then the share of each of the remaining persons increased by:**

- **A.** 1 7  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 1 8
- **C.** 1 9
- **D.** 7 8

**Explanation:** Original share of 1 person = 1 8 New share of 1 person = 1 7 Increase = 1 - 1 = 1 7 8 56 Required fraction = (1/56) = 1 x 8 = 1 (1/8) 56 1 7

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002)*

---

**Q313. The price of 10 chairs is equal to that of 4 tables. The price of 15 chairs and 2 tables together is Rs. 4000. The total price of 12 chairs and 3 tables is:**

- **A.** Rs. 3500
- **B.** Rs. 3750
- **C.** Rs. 3840
- **D.** Rs. 3900  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the cost of a chair and that of a table be Rs. x and Rs. y respectively. Then, 10 x = 4 y or y = 5 x . 2 15 x + 2 y = 4000 15 x + 2 x 5 x = 4000 2 20 x = 4000 x = 200. So, y = 5 x 200 = 500. 2 Hence, the cost of 12 chairs and 3 tables = 12 x + 3 y = Rs. (2400 + 1500) = Rs. 3900.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/)*

---

**Q314. (469 + 174) 2 - (469 - 174) 2 = ? (469 x 174)**

- **A.** 2
- **B.** 4  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 295
- **D.** 643

**Explanation:** Given exp. = ( a + b ) 2 - ( a - b ) 2 ab = 4 ab ab = 4 (where a = 469, b = 174.)

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003)*

**Q315. One-third of Rahul's savings in National Savings Certificate is equal to one-half of his savings in Public Provident Fund. If he has Rs. 1,50,000 as total savings, how much has he saved in Public Provident Fund ?**

- **A.** Rs. 30,000
- **B.** Rs. 50,000
- **C.** Rs. 60,000  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 90,000

**Explanation:** Let savings in N.S.C and P.P.F. be Rs. x and Rs. (150000 - x ) respectively. Then, 1 x = 1 (150000 - x ) 3 2 x + x = 75000 3 2 5 x = 75000 6 x = 75000 x 6 = 90000 5 Savings in Public Provident Fund = Rs. (150000 - 90000) = Rs. 60000

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002)*

(ii) Divide equation (i) by 2, we get the below equation. => x + 2y = 800. --- (iii) Now subtract (iii) from (ii) x + 6y = 1600 (-) x + 2y = 800 ---------------- 4y = 800 ---------------- Therefore, y = 200. Now apply value of y in (iii) => x + 2 x 200 = 800 => x + 400 = 800 Therefore x = 400 Solving (i) and (ii) we get x = 400, y = 200. Cost of 12 shirts = Rs. (12 x 200) = Rs. 2400.

**Q318. A sum of Rs. 1360 has been divided among A, B and C such that A gets of what B gets and B gets of what C gets. B's share is:**

- **A.** Rs. 120
- **B.** Rs. 160
- **C.** Rs. 240  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Rs. 300

**Explanation:** Let C's share = Rs. x Then, B's share = Rs. x , A's share = Rs. 2 x x = Rs. x 4 3 4 6 x + x + x = 1360 6 4 17 x = 1360 12 x = 1360 x 12 = Rs. 960 17 Hence, B's share = Rs. 960 = Rs. 240. 4

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002)*

**Q319. A fires 5 shots to B's 3 but A kills only once in 3 shots while B kills once in 2 shots. When B has missed 27 times, A has killed:**

- **A.** 30 birds  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 60 birds
- **C.** 72 birds
- **D.** 90 birds

**Explanation:** Let the total number of shots be x . Then, Shots fired by A = 5 x 8 Shots fired by B = 3 x 8 Killing shots by A = 1 of 5 x = 5 x 3 8 24 Shots missed by B = 1 of 3 x = 3 x 2 8 16 3 x = 27 or x = 27 x 16 = 144. 16 3 Birds killed by A = 5 x = 5 x 144 = 30. 24 24

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002)*

**Q320. There are two examinations rooms A and B. If 10 students are sent from A to B, then the number of students in each room is the same. If 20 candidates are sent from B to A, then the number of students in A is double the number of students in B. The number of students in room A is:**

- **A.** 20
- **B.** 80
- **C.** 100  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 200

**Explanation:** Let the number of students in rooms A and B be x and y respectively. Then, x - 10 = y + 10 x - y = 20 .... (i) and x + 20 = 2( y - 20) x - 2 y = -60 .... (ii) Solving (i) and (ii) we get: x = 100 , y = 80. The required answer A = 100.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/)*

---

**Q321. If a - b = 3 and a 2 + b 2 = 29, find the value of ab.**

- **A.** 10  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 12
- **C.** 15
- **D.** 18

**Explanation:** 2 ab = ( a 2 + b 2 ) - ( a - b ) 2 = 29 - 9 = 20 ab = 10.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/)*

**Q323. There are two examinations rooms A and B. If 10 students are sent from A to B, then the number of students in each room is the same. If 20 candidates are sent from B to A, then the number of students in A is double the number of students in B. The number of students in room A is:**

- **A.** 20
- **B.** 80
- **C.** 100  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 200

**Explanation:** Let the number of students in rooms A and B be x and y respectively. Then, x - 10 = y + 10 x - y = 20 .... (i) and x + 20 = 2( y - 20) x - 2 y = -60 .... (ii) Solving (i) and (ii) we get: x = 100 , y = 80. The required answer A = 100.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001)*

**Q324. The price of 10 chairs is equal to that of 4 tables. The price of 15 chairs and 2 tables together is Rs. 4000. The total price of 12 chairs and 3 tables is:**

- **A.** Rs. 3500
- **B.** Rs. 3750
- **C.** Rs. 3840
- **D.** Rs. 3900  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Let the cost of a chair and that of a table be Rs. x and Rs. y respectively. Then, 10 x = 4 y or y = 5 x . 2 15 x + 2 y = 4000 15 x + 2 x 5 x = 4000 2 20 x = 4000 x = 200. So, y = 5 x 200 = 500. 2 Hence, the cost of 12 chairs and 3 tables = 12 x + 3 y = Rs. (2400 + 1500) = Rs. 3900.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004001)*

---

**Q325. To fill a tank, 25 buckets of water is required. How many buckets of water will be required to fill the same tank if the capacity of the bucket is reduced to two-fifth of its present ?**

- **A.** 10
- **B.** 35
- **C.** 62.5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** Cannot be determined

**Explanation:** Let the capacity of 1 bucket = x . Then, the capacity of tank = 25 x . New capacity of bucket = 2 x 5 Required number of buckets = 25 x (2 x /5) = 25 x x 5 2 x = 125 2 = 62.5

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004002)*

---

**Q326. David gets on the elevator at the 11 th floor of a building and rides up at the rate of 57 floors per minute. At the same time, Albert gets on an elevator at the 51st floor of the same building and rides down at the rate of 63 floors per minute. If they continue travelling at these rates, then at which floor will their paths cross ?**

- **A.** 19
- **B.** 28
- **C.** 30  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 37

**Explanation:** Suppose their paths cross after x minutes. Then, 11 + 57 x = 51 - 63 x 120 x = 40 x = 1 3 Number of floors covered by David in (1/3) min. = 1 x 57 = 19. 3 So, their paths cross at (11 +19) i.e., 30 th floor.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/simplification/004003)*

---

## Numerics: Square Root & Cube Root

- **D.** 87

**Explanation:** (.000216) 1/3 = 216 1/3 10 6 = 6 x 6 x 6 1/3 10 2 x 10 2 x 10 2 = 6 10 2 = 6 100 = 0.06

**Q328. 3 - 1 2 simplifies to: 3**

- **A.** 3 4
- **B.** 4 3
- **C.** 4 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** 3 - 1 2 = ( 3 ) 2 + 1 2 - 2 x 3 x 1 3 3 3 = 3 + 1 - 2 3 = 1 + 1 3 = 4 3

- **B.** 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 4
- **D.** 3 5

**Explanation:** (7 + 3 5 )(7 - 3 5 ) = (7) 2 - (3 5 ) 2 = 49 - 45 = 4 = 2.

**Explanation:** 3 5 + 125 = 17.88 3 5 + 25 x 5 = 17.88 3 5 + 5 5 = 17.88 8 5 = 17.88 5 = 2.235 80 + 6 5 = 16 x 5 + 6 5 = 4 5 + 6 5 = 10 5 = (10 x 2.235) = 22.35

- **D.** 2.1039

**Explanation:** 4 a 2 - 4 a + 1 + 3 a = (1) 2 + (2 a ) 2 - 2 x 1 x 2 a + 3 a = (1 - 2 a ) 2 + 3 a = (1 - 2 a ) + 3 a = (1 + a ) = (1 + 0.1039) = 1.1039

**Q332. The least perfect square, which is divisible by each of 21, 36 and 66 is:**

- **A.** 213444  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 214344
- **C.** 214434
- **D.** 231444

**Explanation:** L.C.M. of 21, 36, 66 = 2772. Now, 2772 = 2 x 2 x 3 x 3 x 7 x 11 To make it a perfect square, it must be multiplied by 7 x 11. So, required number = 2 2 x 3 2 x 7 2 x 11 2 = 213444

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/square-root-and-cube-root/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/square-root-and-cube-root/)*

- **C.** 144
- **D.** 196

- **B.** 13  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 16
- **D.** 17.5

**Q350. If m and n are whole numbers such that m n = 121, the value of ( m - 1) n + 1 is:**

- **A.** 1
- **B.** 10
- **C.** 121
- **D.** 1000  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** We know that 11 2 = 121. Putting m = 11 and n = 2, we get: ( m - 1) n + 1 = (11 - 1) (2 + 1) = 10 3 = 1000.

**Explanation:** 1 + 1 = 1 + 1 1 + a n a m 1 + a m a n 1 + a ( n - m ) 1 + a ( m - n ) = a m + a n ( a m + a n ) ( a m + a n ) = ( a m + a n ) ( a m + a n ) = 1.

**Q366. 1 + 1 + 1 = ? 1 + x ( b - a ) + x ( c - a ) 1 + x ( a - b ) + x ( c - b ) 1 + x ( b - c ) + x ( a - c )**

- **A.** 0
- **B.** 1  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** x a - b - c
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Given Exp. = 1 + 1 + 1 1 + x b + x c x a x a 1 + x a + x c x b x b 1 + x b + x a x c x c = x a + x b + x c ( x a + x b + x c ) ( x a + x b + x c ) ( x a + x b + x c ) = ( x a + x b + x c ) ( x a + x b + x c ) = 1.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/surds-and-indices/016002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/surds-and-indices/016002)*

## Numerics: Time and Work

**Q367. A takes twice as much time as B or thrice as much time as C to finish a piece of work. Working together, they can finish the work in 2 days. B can do the work alone in:**

- **A.** 4 days
- **B.** 6 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 8 days
- **D.** 12 days

**Explanation:** Suppose A, B and C take x , x and x days respectively to finish the work. 2 3 Then, 1 + 2 + 3 = 1 x x x 2 6 = 1 x 2 x = 12. So, B takes (12/2) = 6 days to finish the work.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029005](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029005)*

---

**Q368. A can do a piece of work in 4 hours; B and C together can do it in 3 hours, while A and C together can do it in 2 hours. How long will B alone take to do it?**

- **A.** 8 hours
- **B.** 10 hours
- **C.** 12 hours  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 24 hours

**Explanation:** A's 1 hour's work = 1 ; 4 (B + C)'s 1 hour's work = 1 ; 3 (A + C)'s 1 hour's work = 1 . 2 (A + B + C)'s 1 hour's work = 1 + 1 = 7 . 4 3 12 B's 1 hour's work = 7 - 1 = 1 . 12 2 12 B alone will take 12 hours to do the work.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002)*

---

**Q369. 4 men and 6 women can complete a work in 8 days, while 3 men and 7 women can complete it in 10 days. In how many days will 10 women complete it?**

- **A.** 35
- **B.** 40  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 45
- **D.** 50

**Explanation:** Let 1 man's 1 day's work = x and 1 woman's 1 day's work = y . Then, 4 x + 6 y = 1 and 3 x + 7 y = 1 . 8 10 Solving the two equations, we get: x = 11 , y = 1 400 400 1 woman's 1 day's work = 1 . 400 10 women's 1 day's work = 1 x 10 = 1 . 400 40 Hence, 10 women will complete the work in 40 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029003)*

---

**Q370. P can complete a work in 12 days working 8 hours a day. Q can complete the same work in 8 days working 10 hours a day. If both P and Q work together, working 8 hours a day, in how many days can they complete the work?**

- **A.** 5 5 11  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 5 6 11
- **C.** 6 5 11
- **D.** 6 6 11

**Explanation:** P can complete the work in (12 x 8) hrs. = 96 hrs. Q can complete the work in (8 x 10) hrs. = 80 hrs. P's1 hour's work = 1 and Q's 1 hour's work = 1 . 96 80 (P + Q)'s 1 hour's work = 1 + 1 = 11 . 96 80 480 So, both P and Q will finish the work in 480 hrs. 11 Number of days of 8 hours each = 480 x 1 = 60 days = 5 5 days. 11 8 11 11

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029003)*

---

**Q371. A can do a work in 15 days and B in 20 days. If they work on it together for 4 days, then the fraction of the work that is left is :**

- **A.** 1 4
- **B.** 1 10
- **C.** 7 15
- **D.** 8 15  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** A's 1 day's work = 1 ; 15 B's 1 day's work = 1 ; 20 (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 7 . 15 20 60 (A + B)'s 4 day's work = 7 x 4 = 7 . 60 15 Therefore, Remaining work = 1 - 7 = 8 . 15 15

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001)*

**Q372. In how many days can 10 women finish a work? I. 10 men can complete the work in 6 days. II. 10 men and 10 women together can complete the work in 3 3 days 7 III. If 10 men work for 3 days and thereafter 10 women replace them, the remaining work in completed in 4 days.**

- **A.** Any two of the three  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** I and II only
- **C.** II and III only
- **D.** I and III only

**Explanation:** I. (10 x 6) men can complete the work in 1 day. 1 man's 1 day's work = 1 60 II. 10 x 24 men + 10 x 24 women can complete the work in 1 day. 7 7 240 men's 1 day work + 240 women's 1 day work = 1. 7 7 240 x 1 + 240 women's 1 day's work = 1. 7 60 7 240 women's 1 day's work = 1 - 4 = 3 7 7 7 10 women's 1 day's work = 3 x 7 x 10 = 1 7 240 8 So, 10 women can finish the work in 8 days. III. (10 men's work for 3 days) + (10 women's work for 4 days) = 1 (10 x 3) men's 1 day's work + (10 x 4) women's 1 day's work = 1 30 men's 1 day's work + 40 women's 1 day's work = 1 Thus, I and III will give us the answer. And, II and III will give us the answer. Correct answer is (A).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/031001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/031001)*

**Q373. A is thrice as good as workman as B and therefore is able to finish a job in 60 days less than B. Working together, they can do it in:**

- **A.** 20 days
- **B.** 22 1 days 2  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 25 days
- **D.** 30 days

**Explanation:** Ratio of times taken by A and B = 1 : 3. The time difference is (3 - 1) 2 days while B take 3 days and A takes 1 day. If difference of time is 2 days, B takes 3 days. If difference of time is 60 days, B takes 3 x 60 = 90 days. 2 So, A takes 30 days to do the work. A's 1 day's work = 1 30 B's 1 day's work = 1 90 (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 4 = 2 30 90 90 45 A and B together can do the work in 45 = 22 1 days. 2 2

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001)*

**Q374. X can do a piece of work in 40 days. He works at it for 8 days and then Y finished it in 16 days. How long will they together take to complete the work?**

- **A.** 13 1 days 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 15 days
- **C.** 20 days
- **D.** 26 days

**Explanation:** Work done by X in 8 days = 1 x 8 = 1 . 40 5 Remaining work = 1 - 1 = 4 . 5 5 Now, 4 work is done by Y in 16 days. 5 Whole work will be done by Y in 16 x 5 = 20 days. 4 X's 1 day's work = 1 , Y's 1 day's work = 1 . 40 20 (X + Y)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 3 . 40 20 40 Hence, X and Y will together complete the work in 40 = 13 1 days. 3 3

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029006)*

---

**Q375. A and B can together finish a work 30 days. They worked together for 20 days and then B left. After another 20 days, A finished the remaining work. In how many days A alone can finish the work?**

- **A.** 40
- **B.** 50
- **C.** 54
- **D.** 60  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** (A + B)'s 20 day's work = 1 x 20 = 2 . 30 3 Remaining work = 1 - 2 = 1 . 3 3 Now, 1 work is done by A in 20 days. 3 Therefore, the whole work will be done by A in (20 x 3) = 60 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029003](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029003)*

**Q376. How many workers are required for completing the construction work in 10 days? I. 20% of the work can be completed by 8 workers in 8 days. II. 20 workers can complete the work in 16 days. III. One-eighth of the work can be completed by 8 workers in 5 days.**

- **A.** I only  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II and III only
- **C.** III only
- **D.** I and III only

**Explanation:** I. 20 work can be completed by (8 x 8) workers in 1 day. 100 Whole work can be completed by (8 x 8 x 5) workers in 1 day. = 8 x 8 x 5 workers in 10 days = 32 workers in 10 days. 10 II. (20 x 16) workers can finish it in 1 day. (20 x 16) workers can finish it in 10 days. 10 32 workers can finish it in 10 days. III. 1 work can be completed by (8 x 5) workers in 1 day. 8 Whole work can be completed by (8 x 5 x 8) workers in 1 day. = 8 x 5 x 8 workers in 10 days = 32 workers in 10 days. 10 Any one of the three gives the answer. Correct answer is (E).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/031001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/031001)*

**Q377. A alone can do a piece of work in 6 days and B alone in 8 days. A and B undertook to do it for Rs. 3200. With the help of C, they completed the work in 3 days. How much is to be paid to C?**

- **A.** Rs. 375
- **B.** Rs. 400  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 600
- **D.** Rs. 800

**Explanation:** C's 1 day's work = 1 - 1 + 1 = 1 - 7 = 1 . 3 6 8 3 24 24 A's wages : B's wages : C's wages = 1 : 1 : 1 = 4 : 3 : 1. 6 8 24 C's share (for 3 days) = Rs. 3 x 1 x 3200 = Rs. 400. 24

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/)*

**Q378. A can finish a work in 24 days, B in 9 days and C in 12 days. B and C start the work but are forced to leave after 3 days. The remaining work was done by A in:**

- **A.** 5 days
- **B.** 6 days
- **C.** 10 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 10 1 days 2

**Explanation:** (B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 7 . 9 12 36 Work done by B and C in 3 days = 7 x 3 = 7 . 36 12 Remaining work = 1 - 7 = 5 . 12 12 Now, 1 work is done by A in 1 day. 24 So, 5 work is done by A in 24 x 5 = 10 days. 12 12

**Q379. A does 80% of a work in 20 days. He then calls in B and they together finish the remaining work in 3 days. How long B alone would take to do the whole work?**

- **A.** 23 days
- **B.** 37 days
- **C.** 37  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 40 days

**Explanation:** Whole work is done by A in 20 x 5 = 25 days. 4 Now, 1 - 4 i.e., 1 work is done by A and B in 3 days. 5 5 Whole work will be done by A and B in (3 x 5) = 15 days. A's 1 day's work = 1 , (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 . 25 15 B's 1 day's work = 1 - 1 = 4 = 2 . 15 25 150 75 So, B alone would do the work in 75 = 37 1 days. 2 2

**Q380. A and B together can complete a task in 7 days. B alone can do it in 20 days. What part of the work was carried out by A? I. A completed the job alone after A and B worked together for 5 days. II. Part of the work done by A could have been done by B and C together in 6 days.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** B's 1 day's work = 1 20 (A+ B)'s 1 day's work = 1 7 I. (A + B)'s 5 day's work = 5 7 Remaining work = 1 - 5 = 2 . 7 7 2 work was carried by A. 7 II. is irrelevant. Correct answer is (A).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/030001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/030001)*

**Q381. A and B can do a work in 8 days, B and C can do the same work in 12 days. A, B and C together can finish it in 6 days. A and C together will do it in :**

- **A.** 4 days
- **B.** 6 days
- **C.** 8 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 12 days

**Explanation:** (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 ; 6 (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 ; 8 (B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 . 12 (A + C)'s 1 day's work = 2 x 1 - 1 + 1 6 8 12 = 1 - 5 3 24 = 3 24 = 1 . 8 So, A and C together will do the work in 8 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029006)*

**Q382. A and B can do a job together in 7 days. A is 1 times as efficient as B. The same job can be done by A alone in :**

- **A.** 9 1 days 3

- **C.** 12 1 days 4
- **D.** 16 1 days 3

**Explanation:** (A's 1 day's work) : (B's 1 day's work) = 7 : 1 = 7 : 4. 4 Let A's and B's 1 day's work be 7 x and 4 x respectively. Then, 7 x + 4 x = 1 11 x = 1 x = 1 . 7 7 77 A's 1 day's work = 1 x 7 = 1 . 77 11

**Q383. X and Y can do a piece of work in 20 days and 12 days respectively. X started the work alone and then after 4 days Y joined him till the completion of the work. How long did the work last?**

- **A.** 6 days
- **B.** 10 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 15 days
- **D.** 20 days

**Explanation:** Work done by X in 4 days = 1 x 4 = 1 . 20 5 Remaining work = 1 - 1 = 4 . 5 5 (X + Y)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 8 = 2 . 20 12 60 15 Now, 2 work is done by X and Y in 1 day. 15 So, 4 work will be done by X and Y in 15 x 4 = 6 days. 5 2 5 Hence, total time taken = (6 + 4) days = 10 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029004](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029004)*

**Q384. A and B can do a piece of work in 30 days, while B and C can do the same work in 24 days and C and A in 20 days. They all work together for 10 days when B and C leave. How many days more will A take to finish the work?**

- **A.** 18 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 24 days
- **C.** 30 days
- **D.** 36 days

**Explanation:** 2(A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 + 1 = 15 = 1 . 30 24 20 120 8 Therefore, (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 = 1 . 2 x 8 16 Work done by A, B, C in 10 days = 10 = 5 . 16 8 Remaining work = 1 - 5 = 3 . 8 8 A's 1 day's work = 1 - 1 = 1 . 16 24 48 Now, 1 work is done by A in 1 day. 48 So, 3 work will be done by A in 48 x 3 = 18 days. 8 8

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029005](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029005)*

**Q385. A and B together can do a piece of work in 30 days. A having worked for 16 days, B finishes the remaining work alone in 44 days. In how many days shall B finish the whole work alone?**

- **A.** 30 days
- **B.** 40 days
- **C.** 60 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 70 days

**Explanation:** Let A's 1 day's work = x and B's 1 day's work = y . Then, x + y = 1 and 16 x + 44 y = 1. 30 Solving these two equations, we get: x = 1 and y = 1 60 60 B's 1 day's work = 1 . 60 Hence, B alone shall finish the whole work in 60 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029006](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029006)*

**Q386. Twenty women can do a work in sixteen days. Sixteen men can complete the same work in fifteen days. What is the ratio between the capacity of a man and a woman?**

- **C.** 5 : 3
- **D.** Data inadequate

**Explanation:** (20 x 16) women can complete the work in 1 day. 1 woman's 1 day's work = 1 . 320 (16 x 15) men can complete the work in 1 day. 1 man's 1 day's work = 1 240 So, required ratio = 1 : 1 240 320 = 1 : 1 3 4 = 4 : 3 (cross multiplied)

- **C.** 25 days
- **D.** 30 days

If difference of time is 60 days, B takes 3 x 60 = 90 days. 2 So, A takes 30 days to do the work. **Q393. How long will Machine Y, working alone, take to produce x candles? I. Machine X produces x candles in 5 minutes. II. Machine X and Machine Y working at the same time produce x candles in 2 minutes.**

- **A.** I alone sufficient while II alone not sufficient to answer  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** II alone sufficient while I alone not sufficient to answer
- **C.** Either I or II alone sufficient to answer
- **D.** Both I and II are not sufficient to answer

**Explanation:** I. gives, Machine X produces x candles in 1 min. 5 II. gives, Machine X and Y produce x candles in 1 min. 2 From I and II, Y produces x - x = 3 x candles in 1 min. 2 5 10 3 x candles are produced by Y in 1 min. 10 x candles will be produced by Y in 10 x x min = 10 min. 3 x 3 Thus, I and II both are necessary to get the answer. Correct answer is (E).

**Q394. 10 women can complete a work in 7 days and 10 children take 14 days to complete the work. How many days will 5 women and 10 children take to complete the work?**

**Q395. A machine P can print one lakh books in 8 hours, machine Q can print the same number of books in 10 hours while machine R can print them in 12 hours. All the machines are started at 9 A.M. while machine P is closed at 11 A.M. and the remaining two machines complete work. Approximately at what time will the work (to print one lakh books) be finished ?**

- **A.** 11:30 A.M.
- **B.** 12 noon
- **C.** 12:30 P.M.
- **D.** 1:00 P.M.  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** (P + Q + R)'s 1 hour's work = 1 + 1 + 1 = 37 . 8 10 12 120 Work done by P, Q and R in 2 hours = 37 x 2 = 37 . 120 60 Remaining work = 1 - 37 = 23 . 60 60 (Q + R)'s 1 hour's work = 1 + 1 = 11 . 10 12 60 Now, 11 work is done by Q and R in 1 hour. 60 So, 23 work will be done by Q and R in 60 x 23 = 23 hours 2 hours. 60 11 60 11 So, the work will be finished approximately 2 hours after 11 A.M., i.e., around 1 P.M.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002)*

**Q396. A can do a work in 15 days and B in 20 days. If they work on it together for 4 days, then the fraction of the work that is left is :**

- **A.** 1 4
- **B.** 1 10
- **C.** 7 15
- **D.** 8 15  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** A's 1 day's work = 1 ; 15 B's 1 day's work = 1 ; 20 (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 7 . 15 20 60 (A + B)'s 4 day's work = 7 x 4 = 7 . 60 15 Therefore, Remaining work = 1 - 7 = 8 . 15 15

**Q397. A is 30% more efficient than B. How much time will they, working together, take to complete a job which A alone could have done in 23 days?**

- **A.** 11 days
- **B.** 13 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 20 3 days 17
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Ratio of times taken by A and B = 100 : 130 = 10 : 13. Suppose B takes x days to do the work. Then, 10 : 13 :: 23 : x x = 23 x 13 x = 299 . 10 10 A's 1 day's work = 1 ; 23 B's 1 day's work = 10 . 299 (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 10 = 23 = 1 . 23 299 299 13 Therefore, A and B together can complete the work in 13 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029004](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029004)*

**Q398. A, B and C can do a piece of work in 20, 30 and 60 days respectively. In how many days can A do the work if he is assisted by B and C on every third day?**

- **A.** 12 days
- **B.** 15 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 16 days
- **D.** 18 days

**Explanation:** A's 2 day's work = 1 x 2 = 1 . 20 10 (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 + 1 = 6 = 1 . 20 30 60 60 10 Work done in 3 days = 1 + 1 = 1 . 10 10 5 Now, 1 work is done in 3 days. 5 Whole work will be done in (3 x 5) = 15 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/)*

---

**Q399. A works twice as fast as B. If B can complete a work in 12 days independently, the number of days in which A and B can together finish the work in :**

- **A.** 4 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 6 days
- **C.** 8 days
- **D.** 18 days

**Explanation:** Ratio of rates of working of A and B = 2 : 1. So, ratio of times taken = 1 : 2. B's 1 day's work = 1 . 12 A's 1 day's work = 1 ; (2 times of B's work) 6 (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 3 = 1 . 6 12 12 4 So, A and B together can finish the work in 4 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029005](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029005)*

---

**Q400. A, B and C can complete a piece of work in 24, 6 and 12 days respectively. Working together, they will complete the same work in:**

- **A.** 1 day 24
- **B.** 7 day 24
- **C.** 3 3 days 7  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 4 days

**Explanation:** Formula: If A can do a piece of work in n days, then A's 1 day's work = 1 . n (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 + 1 = 7 . 24 6 12 24 Formula: If A's 1 day's work = 1 , then A can finish the work in n days. n So, all the three together will complete the job in 24 days = 3 3 days. 7 7

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029004](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029004)*

---

**Q401. 8 men and 14 women are working together in a field. After working for 3 days, 5 men and 8 women leave the work. How many more days will be required to complete the work? I. 19 men and 12 women together can complete the work in 18 days. II. 16 men can complete two-third of the work in 16 days. III. In 1 day, the work done by three men in equal to the work done by four women.**

- **A.** I only
- **B.** II only
- **C.** III only
- **D.** I or II or III  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Clearly, I only gives the answer. Similarly, II only gives the answer. And, III only gives the answer. Correct answer is (D).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/032001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/032001)*

---

**Q402. A alone can do a piece of work in 6 days and B alone in 8 days. A and B undertook to do it for Rs. 3200. With the help of C, they completed the work in 3 days. How much is to be paid to C?**

- **A.** Rs. 375
- **B.** Rs. 400  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** Rs. 600
- **D.** Rs. 800

**Explanation:** C's 1 day's work = 1 - 1 + 1 = 1 - 7 = 1 . 3 6 8 3 24 24 A's wages : B's wages : C's wages = 1 : 1 : 1 = 4 : 3 : 1. 6 8 24 C's share (for 3 days) = Rs. 3 x 1 x 3200 = Rs. 400. 24

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001)*

---

**Q403. If 6 men and 8 boys can do a piece of work in 10 days while 26 men and 48 boys can do the same in 2 days, the time taken by 15 men and 20 boys in doing the same type of work will be:**

- **A.** 4 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 5 days
- **C.** 6 days
- **D.** 7 days

**Explanation:** Let 1 man's 1 day's work = x and 1 boy's 1 day's work = y . Then, 6 x + 8 y = 1 and 26 x + 48 y = 1 . 10 2 Solving these two equations, we get : x = 1 and y = 1 . 100 200 (15 men + 20 boy)'s 1 day's work = 15 + 20 = 1 . 100 200 4 15 men and 20 boys can do the work in 4 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002)*

---

**Q404. A can lay railway track between two given stations in 16 days and B can do the same job in 12 days. With help of C, they did the job in 4 days only. Then, C alone can do the job in:**

- **A.** 9 1 days 5
- **B.** 9 2 days 5
- **C.** 9 3 days 5  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 10

**Explanation:** (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 , 4 A's 1 day's work = 1 , 16 B's 1 day's work = 1 . 12 C's 1 day's work = 1 - 1 + 1 = 1 - 7 = 5 . 4 16 12 4 48 48 So, C alone can do the work in 48 = 9 3 days. 5 5

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001)*

---

**Q405. A can do a certain work in the same time in which B and C together can do it. If A and B together could do it in 10 days and C alone in 50 days, then B alone could do it in:**

- **A.** 15 days
- **B.** 20 days
- **C.** 25 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 30 days

**Explanation:** (A + B)'s 1 day's work = 1 10 C's 1 day's work = 1 50 (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 = 6 = 3 . .... (i) 10 50 50 25 A's 1 day's work = (B + C)'s 1 day's work .... (ii) From (i) and (ii), we get: 2 x (A's 1 day's work) = 3 25 A's 1 day's work = 3 . 50 B's 1 day's work 1 - 3 = 2 = 1 . 10 50 50 25 So, B alone could do the work in 25 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029002)*

---

**Q406. A, B and C can do a piece of work in 20, 30 and 60 days respectively. In how many days can A do the work if he is assisted by B and C on every third day?**

- **A.** 12 days
- **B.** 15 days  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 16 days
- **D.** 18 days

**Explanation:** A's 2 day's work = 1 x 2 = 1 . 20 10 (A + B + C)'s 1 day's work = 1 + 1 + 1 = 6 = 1 . 20 30 60 60 10 Work done in 3 days = 1 + 1 = 1 . 10 10 5 Now, 1 work is done in 3 days. 5 Whole work will be done in (3 x 5) = 15 days.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001](https://www.indiabix.com/aptitude/time-and-work/029001)*

## Reasoning: Alpha-Numeric Reasoning

**Q407. c _ bbb _ _ abbbb _ abbb _**

- **A.** aabcb
- **B.** abccb  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** abacb
- **D.** baebb

**Explanation:** The series is c a bbb b / c abbbb/ c abbb b . Thus, the pattern 'cabbbb' is repeated.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077002)*

---

**Q408. U, B, I, P, W, ?**

- **A.** D  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** F
- **C.** Q
- **D.** Z

**Explanation:** The sequence follows a pattern based on the alphabetical positions of the letters, where each letter is positioned at increasingly larger intervals: U (21st) → B (2nd, gap of 6) → I (9th, gap of 7) → P (16th, gap of 7) → W (23rd, gap of 7) → D (4th, gap of 6, wrapping around). The pattern of gaps is 6-7-7-7-6, making D the correct continuation. Why not the others: F would break the established gap pattern seen in the sequence; Q does not fit the alphabetical interval progression that defines this series; Z fails to complete the cyclical wrapping pattern that allows letters to return to earlier positions in the alphabet.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076007](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076007)*

---

**Q409. _bcc _ ac _ aabb _ ab _ cc**

- **A.** aabca
- **B.** abaca
- **C.** bacab  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** bcaca

**Explanation:** The series is b bcc a a/c c aabb/ a ab b cc. Thus, the letter pairs move in a cyclic order.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077005](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077005)*

---

**Q410. 1, 1, 2, 6, 24, ?, 720**

- **A.** 100
- **B.** 104
- **C.** 108
- **D.** 120  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The pattern is x 1, x 2, x 3, x 4,..... So, missing term = 24 x 5 = 120.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074001)*

---

**Q411. In the series 2, 6, 18, 54, ...... what will be the 8th term ?**

- **A.** 4370
- **B.** 4374  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 7443
- **D.** 7434

**Explanation:** Clearly, 2 x 3 = 6, 6 x 3 = 18, 18 x 3 = 54,..... So, the series is a G.P. in which a = 2, r = 3. Therefore 8th term = ar 8-1 = ar 7 = 2 x 3 7 = (2 x 2187) = 4374.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/)*

---

**Q412. _ tu _ rt _ s _ _ usrtu _**

- **A.** rtusru
- **B.** rsutrr
- **C.** rsurtr
- **D.** rsurts  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The series r tu s /rt u s/ rt us/rtu s . Thus, the pattern 'rtus' is repeated.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077001)*

---

**Q413. AB, DEF, HIJK, ?, STUVWX**

- **A.** LMNO
- **B.** LMNOP
- **C.** MNOPQ  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** QRSTU

**Explanation:** The number of letters in the terms of the given series increases by one at each step. The first letter of each term is two steps ahead of the last letter of the preceding term. However, each term consists of consecutive letters in order.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002)*

---

**Q414. Y, B, T, G, O, ?**

- **A.** N
- **B.** M
- **C.** L  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** K

**Explanation:** The given sequence is a combination of two series : I. Y,T, O and II. B, G, ? I consists of 2nd, 7th and 12th letters from the end of the English alphabet, while II consists of 2nd, 7th and 12th letters from the beginning of the English alphabet. So, the missing letter in II is the 12th letter from the beginning of the English alphabet, which is L.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002)*

---

**Q415. ajs, gpy, ?, sbk, yhq**

- **A.** dmv
- **B.** mve  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** oua
- **D.** qzi

**Explanation:** This is a letter sequence pattern where each term shifts by a consistent number of positions in the alphabet. Moving from ajs to gpy involves +6 positions for each letter (a→g, j→p, s→y), and the pattern continues with the same +6 shift: gpy (+6) → mve (+6) → sbk (+6) → yhq. Option (B) mve is correct as it maintains this arithmetic progression pattern. Why not the others: (A) dmv would represent a +3 shift instead of +6, breaking the pattern; (C) oua would represent a +7 shift, which is inconsistent with the established +6 interval; (D) qzi would represent a +9 shift, also deviating from the consistent pattern.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002)*

---

**Q416. A, G, L, P, S, ?**

- **A.** U  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** W
- **C.** X
- **D.** Y

**Explanation:** The sequence follows a pattern where each letter's position in the alphabet increases by 6: A(1) → G(7) → L(12) → P(16) → S(19) → U(21). Each step adds 6 to the position value, making U the correct answer. Why not the others: (B) W would represent a +7 increment, breaking the consistent +6 pattern; (C) X follows a +8 increment from S, which doesn't match the established sequence; (D) Y represents a +9 increment, which also deviates from the +6 rule throughout the series.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076002)*

---

**Q417. A, CD, GHI, ?, UVWXY**

- **A.** LMNO
- **B.** MNO
- **C.** MNOP  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** NOPQ

**Explanation:** Each term consists of consecutive letters in order. The number of letters in the terms goes on increasing by one at each step. Also, there is a gap of one letter between the last letter of the first term and the first letter of the second term; a gap of two letters between the last letter of the second term and the first letter of the third term; and so on. So, there should be a gap of three letters between the last letter of the third term and the first letter of the desired term.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076007](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076007)*

---

**Q418. _ op _ mo _ n _ _ pnmop _.**

- **A.** mnpmon  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** mpnmop
- **C.** mnompn
- **D.** mnpomn

**Explanation:** The series is m op n /mo p n/ mo pn/mop n . Thus, the pattern 'mopn' is repeated.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077005](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/077005)*

**Q419. 120, 99, 80, 63, 48, ?**

- **A.** 35  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 38
- **C.** 39
- **D.** 40

**Explanation:** The pattern is - 21, - 19, - 17, - 15,..... So, missing term = 48 - 13 = 35.

**Q420. 5824, 5242, ?, 4247, 3823**

- **A.** 4467
- **B.** 4718  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 4856
- **D.** 5164

**Explanation:** Each term in the series is obtained by subtracting from the preceding term the number formed by the first three digits of the preceding term. So, missing term = 5242 - 524 = 4718.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074001)*

**Q421. 8, 13, 21, 32, 47, 63, 83**

- **A.** 13
- **B.** 21
- **C.** 32
- **D.** 47  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The correct pattern is + 5, + 8, + 11, + 14,..... So, 47 is wrong and must be replaced by (32 + 14) i.e. 46.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/075001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/075001)*

- **B.** 65423
- **C.** 89654
- **D.** 96542  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The digits are removed one by one from the beginning and the end in order alternately so as to obtain the subsequent terms of the series.

**Q425. 2, 15, 4, 12, 6, 7, ?, ?**

- **A.** 8, 8
- **B.** 8, 0  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 3, 8
- **D.** None of these

**Explanation:** Let the missing terms of the series be x 1 and x 2 . Thus, the sequence 2, 15, 4, 12, 6, 7, x 1 x 2 is a combination of two series : I. 2, 4, 6, x 1 and II. 15, 12, 7, x 2 I consists of consecutive even numbers. So, missing term, x 1 = 8. The pattern in II is - 3, - 5,......So, missing term, x 2 = 7 - 7 = 0.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074001)*

**Q435. H, I, K, N, ?**

- **A.** O
- **B.** Q
- **C.** R  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** S

**Explanation:** The sequence follows a pattern where each letter is separated by an increasing number of letters in the alphabet: H to I (skip 0), I to K (skip 1), K to N (skip 2), N to R (skip 3). Therefore, R is the correct answer. Why not the others: (A) O would represent a skip of only 1 letter, breaking the pattern; (B) Q would represent a skip of 2 letters, repeating a previous interval instead of increasing; (D) S would represent a skip of 4 letters, which exceeds the expected increment of 3.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076001)*

**Q438. 5, 2, 7, 9, 16, 25, ?**

- **A.** 41  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 45
- **C.** 48
- **D.** 52

**Q440. 1, 2, 4, 8, 16, 32, 64, 96**

- **B.** 32
- **C.** 64
- **D.** 96  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Each term of the series is obtained by multiplying the preceding term by 2. So, 96 is wrong and must be replaced by (64 x 2) i.e. 128.

**Q441. Z, Y, X, U, T, S, P, O, N, K, ?, ?**

- **A.** H,G
- **B.** H, I
- **C.** I,H
- **D.** J, I  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The sequence follows a pattern of skipping backward through the alphabet with varying gaps. Starting from Z and moving backward: Z to Y (skip 0), Y to X (skip 0), X to U (skip 2: V, W), U to T (skip 0), T to S (skip 0), S to P (skip 2: Q, R), P to O (skip 0), O to N (skip 0), N to K (skip 2: L, M). The pattern repeats: after every two consecutive letters, skip 2 letters backward. Following this pattern, K should be followed by J (skip 0), then I (skip 0), giving us J, I. Why not the others: (A) H, G continues skipping when the pattern requires stopping at J and I; (B) H, I has incorrect first letter and breaks the sequence logic; (C) I, H reverses the correct order of the answer.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076007](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076007)*

---

**Q442. 10, 14, 26, 42, 70, ?**

- **A.** 100
- **B.** 102
- **C.** 106
- **D.** 114  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** Each term in the series, except the first two terms, is 2 more than the sum of the preceding two terms. So, missing term = (42 + 70) + 2 = 114.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074006](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074006)*

- **D.** 129  ✅ **(correct answer)**

Why not the others: (B) DM breaks the pattern by using M instead of L; (C) GH does not continue the alphabetical progression from the established sequence; (D) LM skips multiple letters and does not follow the consistent one-letter advancement pattern.

**Q460. WFB, TGD, QHG, ?**

- **A.** NIJ
- **B.** NIK  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** NJK
- **D.** OIK

**Explanation:** This is a letter sequence pattern where each term shifts backwards in the alphabet. WFB→TGD moves back 3 positions (W→T, F→G, B→D), TGD→QHG moves back 3 positions (T→Q, G→H, D→G), and QHG→NIK follows the same pattern, moving back 3 positions (Q→N, H→I, G→K). Why not the others: (A) NIJ incorrectly applies the pattern to only some letters; (C) NJK shifts the middle letter incorrectly (H→J instead of H→I); (D) OIK starts with O instead of N (Q moved back 3 is N, not O).

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076001)*

---

**Q461. 3, 8, 13, 24, 41, ?**

- **A.** 70  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 75
- **C.** 80
- **D.** 85

**Explanation:** The pattern followed is : nth term + (n + l)th term + (n + 1) = (n + 2)th term. Thus, 1st term + 2nd term + 2 = 3rd term; 2nd term + 3rd term + 3 = 4th term and so on. So, missing term = 6th term = 4th term + 5th term + 5 = 24 + 41 + 5 = 70.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074006](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/074006)*

---

**Q462. 5, 6, 9, 15, ?, 40**

- **A.** 21
- **B.** 25  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 27
- **D.** 33

**Explanation:** The pattern is + 1, + 3, + 6,....., i.e. + 1, + (1 + 2), + (1 + 2 + 3),..... So, missing term = 15 + (1 + 2 + 3 + 4) = 25.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/073002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/073002)*

**Q478. In the series 2, 6, 18, 54, ...... what will be the 8th term ?**

- **A.** 4370
- **B.** 4374  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 7443
- **D.** 7434

**Explanation:** Clearly, 2 x 3 = 6, 6 x 3 = 18, 18 x 3 = 54,..... So, the series is a G.P. in which a = 2, r = 3. Therefore 8th term = ar 8-1 = ar 7 = 2 x 3 7 = (2 x 2187) = 4374.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/073001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/073001)*

---

**Q479. AZ, GT, MN, ?, YB**

- **A.** JH
- **B.** SH  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** SK
- **D.** TS

**Explanation:** The pattern follows a sequence where each pair's letters are positioned at regular intervals in the alphabet. In AZ (1st and 26th letters), GT (7th and 20th), MN (13th and 14th), the first letter advances by 6 positions each time (A→G→M→S), while the second letter decreases by 6 positions (Z→T→N→H), making SH the correct answer. Why not the others: (A) JH places the first letter too early in the sequence; (C) SK breaks the decreasing pattern for the second letter; (D) TS reverses the expected direction of the first letter's progression.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/series-completion/076001)*

---

- **B.** 10201

**Explanation:** Each term in the series is obtained by adding 1 to the square of the preceding term. So, missing term = (101) 2 + 1 = 10202.

## Reasoning: Analogy

**Q482. 27 : 125 :: 64 : ?**

- **A.** 162
- **B.** 216  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** 517
- **D.** 273

**Explanation:** 27 → 3 3 ; 125 → 5 3 ; 64 → 4 3 Therefore ? = 6 3 = 216.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/037004](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/037004)*

---

**Q483. K/T : 11/20 :: J/R : ?**

- **A.** 10/18  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 11/19
- **C.** 10/8
- **D.** 9/10

**Explanation:** In Eq. alphabets positions of K and T are 11 and 20 respectively. Similarly positions of J and R are 10 and 18.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/037004](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/037004)*

---

**Q484. Select a suitable figure from the Answer Figures that would replace the question mark (?). Problem Figures: Answer Figures: (A) (B) (C) (D) (1) (2) (3) (4) (5)**

- **A.** 1  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 2
- **C.** 3
- **D.** 4

**Explanation:** The number of sides in the main figure reduces by one; the two circles present inside it, move outside and reach the positions on either side of this figure; a new black circle appears inside the figure.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/non-verbal-reasoning/analogy/004009](https://www.indiabix.com/non-verbal-reasoning/analogy/004009)*

---

**Q485. Peacock : India :: Bear : ?**

- **A.** Australia
- **B.** America
- **C.** Russia  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** England

**Explanation:** As Peacock is the national bird of India, similarly Bear is the national animal of Russia.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/)*

---

**Q486. 335 : 216 :: 987 : ?**

- **A.** 868  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 867
- **C.** 872
- **D.** 888

**Explanation:** As 335 - 216 = 119 Similarly, 987 - X = 119 Therefore, X = 987 - 119 = 868.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/037002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/037002)*

---

**Q487. Kick : Football**

- **A.** Wash : Dishes
- **B.** Dust : Rage
- **C.** Mop : Sweep
- **D.** Throw : Ring  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** As Kick is in the game of Football, similarly Throw is used in the game of Ring.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/038002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/038002)*

---

**Q488. Select a suitable figure from the Answer Figures that would replace the question mark (?). Problem Figures: Answer Figures: (A) (B) (C) (D) (1) (2) (3) (4) (5)**

- **A.** 1
- **B.** 2
- **C.** 3  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** 4

**Explanation:** The upper part of the figure gets vertically inverted.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/non-verbal-reasoning/analogy/004004](https://www.indiabix.com/non-verbal-reasoning/analogy/004004)*

---

**Q489. Select a suitable figure from the Answer Figures that would replace the question mark (?). Problem Figures: Answer Figures: (A) (B) (C) (D) (1) (2) (3) (4) (5)**

- **A.** 1  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** 2
- **C.** 3
- **D.** 4

**Explanation:** The pentagon gets vertically inverted. The lower half of the black element becomes white and this element moves inside the pentagon and gets attached to its upper end.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/non-verbal-reasoning/analogy/003003](https://www.indiabix.com/non-verbal-reasoning/analogy/003003)*

---

**Q490. Lock, Shut, Fasten**

- **A.** Window
- **B.** Door
- **C.** Iron
- **D.** Block  ✅ **(correct answer)**

**Explanation:** The synonym of Lock, Shut and Fasten is Block.

**Q493. Corden : zrogbq :: ? : pxivro**

- **A.** mulmul
- **B.** sulsul  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** munmun
- **D.** srspql

**Explanation:** This is an analogy question involving letter substitution or cipher patterns. In the pair 'Corden : zrogbq', each letter in 'Corden' is transformed to produce 'zrogbq' through a consistent shifting rule (specifically, a reverse alphabet substitution where A↔Z, B↔Y, C↔X, etc.). Applying the same transformation to the missing word produces 'sulsul', which matches option (B). Why not the others: (A) mulmul does not follow the same letter substitution pattern as shown in the Corden example; (C) munmun also fails to match the required transformation rule; (D) srspql contains letters and patterns inconsistent with applying the cipher to any standard word.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036002)*

**Q498. ABCD : WXYZ :: EFGH : ?**

- **A.** STUV  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** ZYXW
- **C.** VUTS
- **D.** WXZY

**Explanation:** In this analogy, ABCD corresponds to WXYZ by reversing the alphabet sequence—each letter maps to its reverse position (A↔Z, B↔Y, C↔X, D↔W). Applying the same reverse-alphabet rule to EFGH gives STUV (E↔V, F↔U, G↔T, H↔S, then arranged in order). Why not the others: (B) ZYXW is simply WXYZ reversed, not the correct reverse-alphabet mapping of EFGH; (C) VUTS is the reverse-alphabet set but in descending order rather than ascending; (D) WXZY is a rearrangement that doesn't follow the consistent reverse-alphabet pattern.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036005](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036005)*

**Q500. AZBY : CXDW :: EVFU : ?**

- **A.** GTHS  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **B.** GHTS
- **C.** GSTH
- **D.** TGSH

**Explanation:** In this analogy, each letter in the first pair follows a pattern where it shifts by 2 positions in the alphabet both forwards and backwards alternately. For AZBY : CXDW, A→C (+2), Z→X (−2), B→D (+2), Y→W (−2). Applying the same pattern to EVFU: E→G (+2), V→T (−2), F→H (+2), U→S (−2) gives GTHS. Why not the others: (B) reverses the order of the last two letters, breaking the pattern; (C) incorrectly places S before T by misapplying the alternating shift; (D) scrambles the letters entirely and doesn't follow the systematic progression.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036001)*

**Q517. ZRYQ : KCJB :: PWOV : ?**

- **A.** GBHA
- **B.** ISJT
- **C.** ELDK  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **D.** EOFP

**Explanation:** The pattern involves shifting each letter backwards by a fixed number of positions in the alphabet. In ZRYQ : KCJB, each letter shifts back by 15 positions (Z→K, R→C, Y→J, Q→B). Applying the same 15-position backward shift to PWOV yields: P→E, W→L, O→D, V→K, giving ELDK. Why not the others: (A) GBHA uses inconsistent or incorrect shift values; (B) ISJT results from forward shifts rather than backward shifts; (D) EOFP applies a different shift pattern that doesn't match the established rule.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036001](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/036001)*

**Q534. NATION : ANTINO :: HUNGRY : ?**

- **A.** HNUGRY
- **B.** UHNGYR  ✅ **(correct answer)**
- **C.** YRNGUH
- **D.** UNHGYR

**Explanation:** In this analogy, NATION is rearranged to ANTINO by moving the first letter (N) to the third position, creating a specific letter-shifting pattern. Applying the same rearrangement pattern to HUNGRY—moving the first letter (H) to the third position—produces UHNGRY, which matches option (B). Why not the others: (A) HNUGRY merely reverses adjacent letters rather than following the systematic positional shift pattern; (C) YRNGUH appears to reverse the entire word, which doesn't match the demonstrated transformation rule; (D) UNHGYR incorrectly repositions letters and doesn't apply the consistent pattern shown in the NATION example.

*Source: [https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/035002](https://www.indiabix.com/verbal-reasoning/analogy/035002)*
